whose virtue and power are lofty and mysterious, resplendent above and below. They have amassed boundless merit, benefiting both the manifest and the hidden. Recently, they have vowed to spread goodness, crafting sacred talismans to relieve the suffering of all, regardless of rank or station, bestowing them without reserve. Yet their responsiveness depends on the sincerity—or lack thereof—of the supplicant.

If one approaches with reverence, purification, focus, and unwavering sincerity, the divine response will be swift, like an echo following a sound. But if one is negligent, insincere, or doubtful, not only will there be no resonance, but the gods will withhold their protection. Few who act thus shall attain peace and good fortune. Devout believers must therefore be ever vigilant, maintaining single-minded devotion, unflagging resolve, and unwavering reverence for the divine. Then, whatever they pray for shall surely receive a response.

Thus it is said: with sincerity, there are gods; without sincerity, there are no gods. How can one not be reverent? How can one not be cautious?

On the tenth day of the third month in the seventeenth year of the Yongle reign.

**Imperially Composed Preface to the *Scripture of the Wondrous Merit of the True Lords of Vast Grace and Numinous Aid, as Spoken by the Heavenly Worthy of Numinous Treasure***

I reflect upon the Dao as teaching: it reveals the profound mysteries of the primordial chaos and the void’s subtlety, embodying the wondrous spontaneity of the Boundless. Dim and obscure, silent and still—gazing, one sees not its form; listening, one hears not its sound. Above, it subtly upholds the imperial order; below, it benefits and succors all beings. Its virtue and power are so vast they defy description.

Among its manifestations are the Great Immortal of the Nine Heavens’ Golden Palace, Illuminator of the Dao and Perfector of Virtue, Revealer of Numinous Might, Universally Beneficent, Pure and Subtle, Cavernously Mysterious, Serenely Void, Wondrously Responsive, Compassionate and Kind, Protector of the Realm and Shelter of the People—the True Lord of Vast Grace, King Jiang; and the Supreme Immortal of the Nine Heavens’ Jade Palace, Propagator of Transformation and Upholder of the Teachings, Radiant in Numinous Might, Vastly Beneficent, Lofty and Luminous, Magnanimous and Tranquil, Serenely Profound, Wondrously Responsive, Benevolent and Kind, Assistant to the Realm and Guardian of the People—the True Lord of Direct Grace, King Rao. Their spirits are refined and their excellence divinely endowed, their natures marked by magnanimity, kindness, and compassion. They cherish the people and love all creatures, are loyal to their lords and filial to their parents, and revere the Three Treasures.

Firm in resolve and devoted to goodness, single-minded in diligence and unwavering in purpose, their merits perfected and conduct fulfilled, they thus received celestial investiture, bestowed with illustrious titles, and ranked among the immortals. Assisting and illuminating the mechanisms of transformation, they emerge from darkness into light, warding off disasters and repelling calamities, dispelling misfortune to usher in auspiciousness. Spreading protection across the earth, they benefit and succor all living beings.

Of late, they have magnified their numinous blessings, safeguarding and shielding Our person, upholding and sheltering Us, thereby securing peace and tranquility. Thereafter, they manifested talismanic remedies, widely bestowing them upon the realm, with the aim of enabling people to purge illness and suffering and to flourish in progeny. Their great virtue and profound grace are equal to heaven and earth. Moved by the favor of the spirits, We have never forgotten, even for a moment.

Amidst the myriad affairs of state, We perused the *Marvelous Scripture of the True Lords of Vast Grace and Direct Grace, Spoken by the Numinous Treasure Heavenly Worthy*, wherein the subtle and profound mysteries and unfathomable divine transformations are revealed. Offering expedient benefits and boundless deliverance, it is truly the sun and moon illuminating the dark, the boat and oar crossing the sea. Thus, We have had it carved and printed to widely disseminate it, in repayment of the spirits’ protection.

Virtuous and faithful devotees who purify themselves through repentance, revere the Three Treasures, fulfill loyalty and filial piety, practice benevolence and righteousness, and earnestly vow to receive, uphold, recite, and chant this scripture shall find their households blessed with fortune, their destinies smooth and prosperous, their descendants flourishing, disasters averted, calamities overcome, and blessings and longevity increased, extending even to their nine generations, all attaining transcendence and ascent.

Should any, however, slander or belittle, slight or disregard the Three Treasures, fail in loyalty or filial piety, lack benevolence or righteousness, and neglect reverent faith and devotion, they shall incur karmic retribution, their households decline and wither, their descendants grow weak and feeble, their lifespans cut short, and their nine generations burdened, forever sinking into the dark abyss. Looking back upon the past, clear evidence abounds.

Alas! Fortune and misfortune, good and evil—all are fashioned by the heart. To do good is to gain blessings; to do evil is to suffer calamity. Such is the natural principle. Thus it is said: "The family that accumulates goodness shall surely have abundant blessings. The family that accumulates evil shall surely have abundant misfortune." It is also said: "Only the August Heaven does not favor the constant; it bestows a hundred blessings upon those who do good and a hundred calamities upon those who do evil." Observing this, how can one fail to be exhorted? How can one fail to be exhorted?

On the first day of the first lunar month in the eighteenth year of the Yongle reign.

---

*The Marvelous Scripture of the True Lords of Vast Grace and Direct Grace, Spoken by the Numinous Treasure Heavenly Worthy*

At that time, the Numinous Treasure Heavenly Worthy was in the Fivefold Luminosity Palace atop the Great Brahma Heaven, seated with a table before Him. Bells and chimes sounded of themselves as He convened the hosts of stellar deities and the great gods of the Five Dipper Stars to expound the Supreme, Boundless, Utmost True and Marvelous Dao.

Then the two envoys of the Dipper’s Central Water, one holding a green staff and the other wielding a yellow axe, stood in attendance before the Emperor. Bowing their heads in reverence, they knelt and addressed Him: "We, Your servants, were fortunate in past lives to encounter the heavenly and human realms. Gazing down upon the sentient beings of the Desire Realm, we see that they are neither loyal nor filial, neither righteous nor benevolent, committing many evil deeds without shame or remorse. The reckoning has reached its end, and this life is the final kalpa. The *Chou Kou Fu Tu* is in disarray, the moral order is fractured, warfare and conflagration rage unchecked, jade and stone alike are consumed in the flames. Some suffer from floods, others from famine. Punishments and taxes are oppressive, plagues and poisons spread. Afflicted by manifold sufferings, they know not how to awaken. The breath of life is nearly extinguished, and the human way is on the verge of collapse. By what karmic conditions may they be saved? We beseech Your compassion to open the gate of expedient means."

The Heavenly Worthy said: "Excellent, excellent! The beings of the final kalpa are like newborn babes. If you are moved by this heart, all shall follow Our teachings. Widely expound the karmic conditions to all beings, enabling them to awaken their natures and cast aside doubt and hesitation. Loyalty and filial piety, benevolence and righteousness—cultivating these four shall ever dwell in fortune and blessings."

The envoys, having received this decree, dared not fail to comply. Thus, in the year of *jiachen* and the year of *bingwu*, they divided their forms to teach and transform, descending into the human realm. Their work accomplished in the Eastern Sea, their traces manifested in the Southern Regions. After a full cycle of sixty years, they returned to their duties. In one region, their incense fire endured for many years, until they encountered the time of extinction, yet they renewed their vows as before. Ascending the immortal ranks, they were bestowed the title of True Lords. By the Heavenly Worthy’s compassion and the Supreme’s virtue of cherishing life, all good men and women come to know that body, nature, and destiny all depend upon the Dao for their arising. Through loyalty, filial piety, benevolence, and righteousness, they comprehend these causes.

On the Three Primes, the Eight Festivals, the Three Assemblies, the Five Fasts, the *gengshen* and *jiazi* days, and one’s own life-day, they burn incense, observe purification, and make offerings according to the rites. With minds turned toward the north, they bow their heads in reverence and recite the names of the True Lords:

The Supreme Immortal of the Nine Heavens’ Golden Palace, Illuminator of the Dao and Attainer of Virtue, Great Transcendent Manifest in Numinous Might, Vastly Beneficent, Subtly Mysterious, Serenely Void, Wondrously Responsive, Compassionate and Kind, Protector of the Realm and Shelter of the People—#1 the True Lord of Vast Grace, King Jiang;

The Supreme Immortal of the Nine Heavens’ Jade Palace, Propagator of Transformation and Upholder of the Teachings, Radiant in Numinous Might, Vastly Beneficent, Lofty and Luminous, Magnanimous and Tranquil, Serenely Profound, Wondrously Responsive, Benevolent and Kind, Assistant to the Realm and Guardian of the People—#2 the True Lord of Direct Grace, King Rao.

Reverently facing the sacred presence, they repent according to the scripture, never violating the True Lords’ vows, and establish themselves through loyalty, filial piety, benevolence, and righteousness. Within, this may increase blessings and extend years; without, it may dispel disasters and overcome calamities. Above, it may enable the souls of ancestors to ascend; below, it may bring peace and prosperity to households. Universally, it is wished that all beings partake in benefit and joy.

Thereupon, the Heavenly Worthy further expounded to the True Lords, speaking in verse:

The True Lords of Vast Grace,
Cultivated truth and attained the Dao.
Roaming and feasting in the immortal realms,
The Heavenly Worthy bestowed Their titles.
The Northern Dipper sent forth Their spirits,
Abundantly present at the left.
Below, They oversee the Three Realms;
Above, They pay homage to the Five Elders.
Blessing the realm and pacifying households,
Their merit is vast.
No prayer goes unanswered,
Silently responding to supplications.
Loyalty, filial piety, benevolence, and righteousness—
Ever the treasures of the self.
Use them as karmic conditions,
Never violate the vows.
All good and evil
Are fashioned by the heart.
Those who do good gain blessings;
Those who do evil suffer calamity.
Swiftly, swiftly, in accordance with the Heavenly Worthy’s ordinance and command!

Here ends *The Marvelous Scripture of the True Lords of Vast Grace and Direct Grace, Spoken by the Numinous Treasure Heavenly Worthy*.

By Heaven’s Mandate and Decree,

Embracing Heaven’s charge and perpetuating the grand design, the Emperor proclaims:

We, having received the Mandate of Heaven, succeed in upholding the vast enterprise. Among the statutes of the state, the rites of sacrifice hold paramount importance. For those whose merit and virtue have benefited the people, and whose numinous power endures through the ages, solemn temples are established in their honor, and the rites of praise and veneration are augmented in due course.

The Most High Golden Portal of the Nine Heavens, Great Immortal of Illuminated Dao and Penetrating Virtue, Manifest Spirit of Vast Salvation, Pure and Subtle, Cavernous and Mysterious, Serene and Void, Wondrously Responsive, Compassionate and Benevolent, Protector of the State and Shelter of the People, Venerable Lord of Vast Grace—born a person of renown, transformed into a radiant deity—during the reign of Our Ancestors, manifested the marvel of profound resonance, answering every prayer. Especially manifest in this age, We hereby confer an additional title:

The Most High Golden Portal of the Nine Heavens, Great Immortal of Illuminated Dao and Penetrating Virtue, Manifest Spirit of Vast Salvation, Pure and Subtle, Cavernous and Mysterious, Serene and Void, Wondrously Responsive, Compassionate and Benevolent, Protector of the State and Shelter of the People, Venerable Lord of Vast Grace and Exalted Blessing.

With reverence, We present the seal and insignia, further magnifying the divine transformation to bless Our August Ming.

On the ninth day of the fourth month, the tenth year of the Xuande era.

Embracing Heaven’s charge and perpetuating the grand design, the Emperor proclaims:

We, having received the Mandate of Heaven, succeed in upholding the vast enterprise. Among the statutes of the state, the rites of sacrifice hold paramount importance. For those whose merit and virtue have benefited the people, and whose numinous power endures through the ages, solemn temples are established in their honor, and the rites of praise and veneration are augmented in due course.

The Jade Portal of the Nine Heavens, Proclaiming Transformation and Upholding the Teachings, Supreme Immortal of Radiant Spirit and Vast Salvation, Lofty and Illuminated, Vast and Tranquil, Serene and Profound, Wondrously Responsive, Benevolent and Compassionate, Assistant to the State and Guardian of the People, Venerable Lord of Vast Grace—born a person of renown, transformed into a radiant deity—during the reign of Our Ancestors, manifested the marvel of profound resonance. Answering every prayer, especially manifest in that era, We hereby confer an additional title:

The Jade Portal of the Nine Heavens, Proclaiming Transformation and Upholding the Teachings, Supreme Immortal of Radiant Spirit and Vast Salvation, Lofty and Illuminated, Vast and Tranquil, Serene and Profound, Wondrously Responsive, Benevolent and Compassionate, Assistant to the State and Guardian of the People, Venerable Lord of Vast Grace and Exalted Blessing.

With reverence, We present the seal and insignia, further magnifying the divine transformation to bless Our August Ming.

On the ninth day of the fourth month, the tenth year of the Xuande era.

Imperially Composed Stele for the Temple of Vast Grace and Numinous Salvation

We have heard that the great virtue of Heaven and Earth is the giving of life. Within the ninefold expanse of their embrace, all living beings—great and small, high and low—are cherished by the heart of Heaven and Earth, which desires that each fulfill its nature, receive its nurture, and not lose its proper place. Moreover, sages, the wise, and heroes of outstanding talent arise to supplement the great work of creation. Thus, the extraordinary merits and mighty deeds of numinous spirits have been renowned through the ages. Those who govern the realm, embodying the heart of Heaven and praising the virtue of the spirits, include them in the sacrificial canon to offer prayers and repayments—this, too, has been recorded through the ages.

Our August Ancestor, the Emperor Taizong Wen, once dreamed of two divine beings who declared they dwelled in the southern seaside and had come to assist the state. The Emperor marveled at this. The following day, an official of rites reported the affairs of the Two Venerable Lords of Numinous Salvation in Min. This precisely matched the dream, so a special envoy was swiftly dispatched with incense to welcome the divine images to Beijing. There, west of the palace city, the Temple of Vast Grace and Numinous Salvation was established to honor them with sacrifices. Their former titles were augmented with illustrious appellations. Truly, the spirits are of utmost benevolence, responding to every prayer.

Theirs is the power to bestow blessings and avert calamities, swift as echo follows sound. What they have accorded with the imperial will is beyond full recounting. Seasonal offerings are made with solemnity and abundance. Our August Ancestor, Emperor Renzong Zhao, and our Imperial Father, Emperor Xuanzong Zhang, both upheld the established rites, honoring them with reverent sacrifices.

We, inheriting the celestial mandate and governing the great treasure of the realm, bear upon Our shoulders the profound grace of Our Sacred Ancestress the Grand Empress Dowager and Our Sacred Mother the Empress Dowager, and pray that their boundless fortune may endure for ten thousand years. Below, We contemplate the deep hopes of the myriad states and peoples under heaven, and pray that all may ascend to prosperity. Yet, mindful of Our own humble virtue, how could We alone be worthy of such resounding trust? Relying upon the will of Our ancestors, We have expanded and exalted the temple halls, reverently honoring the divine might, guiding and welcoming auspicious blessings. Thus, We augment the divine titles as follows:

**Nine Heavens Golden Portal Illuminating Dao and Manifesting Virtue Great Immortal, Radiantly Manifesting, Universally Salvific, Pure and Subtle, Penetrating Mystery, Serene and Void, Wondrously Responsive, Compassionate and Benevolent, Protector of the State and Shelter of the People, Exalter of Blessings, Vastly Gracious Perfected Lord.**

**Nine Heavens Jade Portal Propagating Transformation and Upholding the Dao Supreme Immortal, Illustriously Manifesting, Vastly Salvific, Lofty and Luminous, Vast and Tranquil, Serene and Profound, Wondrously Responsive, Benevolent and Kind, Assistant of the State and Guardian of the People, Bestower of Abundant Blessings, Vastly Gracious Perfected Lord.**

The origins of these deities trace back to ancient roots. They descend from the lineage of Zhuanxu, enfeoffed in the state of Xu, and rendered repeated service to the Xia, Shang, and Zhou dynasties. By the time of King Yan, their cultivation of benevolence and righteousness won the hearts of the people, ensuring the flourishing of their descendants. Through the Han and Tang dynasties, their merits and virtues were repeatedly recorded.

The two divine brothers were sons of the Loyal and Martial Emperor, the Yi Ancestor of the Southern Tang. The elder was enfeoffed as Prince of Jiang, the younger as Prince of Rao. Both were endowed with extraordinary nature, possessing the qualities of benevolence and sagacity, and fulfilling the virtues of loyalty and filial piety. They devoted themselves to the Great Dao, mastering its profound mysteries.

Initially, both were commanded to guard Jinling, where their achievements and virtues flourished, and the people were universally moved and delighted. Later, they were both commanded to lead troops into Min, where their utmost care for the people aligned with the will of heaven. The people cherished and revered them, flocking to them like rain. The people of Min built a shrine to them north of Golden Turtle Peak, where their images were venerated with the reverence due to a stern father.

One day, they addressed the multitude, saying: "Next year, We shall part from you, yet We cannot bear to leave you." When the time came, they departed this world in succession.

Not long after, the spirits descended to speak through mortals, declaring: "Together We have received the August Emperor’s command to assume office in the Dipper Palace, that We may protect the lands below." Thereupon, the people of Min redoubled their reverence in sacrifice, and every prayer met with response.

Beneath the shrine lay a deep pool. In times of drought, when supplicants prayed, a crimson serpent would emerge from the pool, and clouds would rise from its surface, followed by sweet rain pouring down in torrents, ensuring a bountiful harvest. When the Yan Brook swelled with torrential floods, the people, stricken with fear, turned their gaze to the shrine and pleaded for aid. Suddenly, a multitude of laborers appeared, wielding baskets and spades to dredge the waters. The floodwaters receded without causing harm, and the laborers vanished without a trace.

During the Xining era of the Song, when Liu Yi of Min governed Guizhou and repelled the Man bandits, when Han Shizhong fought at Dayi Town, and when Wu Jie battled at Heshang Plain, all achieved victory through the spirits’ assistance. Whether rescuing the people from fire and flood, prolonging their descendants’ lives, or performing extraordinary feats of efficacy, these deeds were all meticulously recorded, their brilliance resplendent and evident.

For the spirits had stored the essence of heaven and earth and received the finest of the Five Phases, thus in life possessing perfect virtue. In death, their luminous efficacy grasped the mechanisms of qi, aiding the mysterious transformations of the Dao, eradicating calamities and malevolent influences for the state and its people, and amassing abundant auspicious blessings. Their glory grew ever more resplendent with the passage of time.

Now, as We inscribe the completion of the shrine’s renovation, We also record the spirits’ lineage and their greatest virtues upon enduring stone, to be preserved for posterity. We append this poem:

Essence of the Two Modes,
Finest of the Five Stars.
Born as sages of wisdom,
Departed as radiant spirits.
Together they blazed in splendor,
Golden elder and jade younger.
Steadfast in filial piety and loyalty,
Their beneficence graced the age.
Riding the whirlwind and clouds,
They returned to the Emperor’s realm.
Their merit aided creation’s nurture,
Their rank equaled the Dipper’s balance.
Looking down in compassion upon the people,
Their gaze unceasing in care.
Averting disasters, warding off harm,
They congealed blessings and bestowed grace.
At Golden Turtle Peak,
The shrine first arose.
Their numinous transformations proclaimed,
A shrine was built in the capital.
August were the Three Saints,
Reverently served as one.
The glory of the spirits,
Bright as the sun’s radiance.
The heir ascends the great throne,
Faithfully upholding the eternal norms.
We refine the sacrificial rites,
To welcome blessings and fortune.
The prosperity of the imperial line,
Protects both family and state.
The flourishing of the supreme principle,
Extends to all people and things.
West of the palace city,
The numinous temple stands.
The imperial destiny and sacred rites,
Shall endure for ten thousand years.

**First Day of the First Month, Zhengtong Era, Year One**

**Eulogy of the Golden Palace**
Great indeed, True Lords,
Endowed with the spirit of rivers and mountains.
Their merit rivals sun and moon,
Their virtue matches heaven and earth.
Numinous in wondrous efficacy,
Upright, wise, and enlightened.
Responding to circumstances, answering prayers,
They vowed to deliver humanity.

**Eulogy of the Jade Palace**
Majestic are the Transcendents above,
Storing the essence of the One and Five.
Their grace descends like rain and dew,
Their might shakes like thunder and lightning.
Numinous efficacy is their nature,
Boundless their blessings and virtue.
Every plea meets with response,
In their vast bestowals, they succor the people.

**True Lords’ Incantation**
True Lords, True Lords,
Great spirits of the Northern Dipper.
They aid heaven and earth’s transformations,
Their brilliance rivals sun and moon.
Below, they govern Fengdu,
Above, they attend the Emperor’s court.
Upholding the true Dharma,
They smite demonic essences.
With the august title *Lingji*,
They bring fortune to all people.
Every prayer meets with response,
Like echo follows sound.
Every plea is answered,
Like shadow follows form.
Those who oppose them perish,
Those who follow them live.
*Om*, Radiant Spirits, Radiant Spirits,
Universally deliver all living beings.
*Qian*, origin, prosperity, benefit, perseverance,
Hasten as the statutes command.
Spirits of Lingji,
Descend swiftly.

**Virtue of Cherishing Life**
Pervades the hearts of the people.
Preserve Our two qi,
Fire yang and water yin.
Dispel disasters, deliver from calamity,
Bless the good, punish the wicked.
Hasten as the statutes command.

**True Lords’ Incantation**
True Lords, True Lords,
Born of the Northern Dipper.
Enacting heaven’s transformations,
Assisting the state and governing the people.
Disseminating the true Dharma,
Smite demonic essences.
Demon kings submit in defense,
The true qi ever abides.
Hasten as the statutes command.

**Marshal’s Incantation**
Marshal’s mighty spirit,
Descend swiftly.
Uphold the true Dharma,
Aid the state and pacify the people.
Discern fortune and misfortune,
Heal illnesses, foretell futures.
Pray for clear skies, beseech for rain,
Smite demonic essences.
Those who follow shall be answered,
Those who oppose shall be punished.
Dispel disasters, bestow blessings,
Ever preserve prosperity.
Hasten as the statutes command.

**Prayer for Clear Skies**
When timely rains fall,
Our millet grows.
Why then this excess,
Floodwaters rampant?
The people suffer in darkness,
Their grievances unvoiced.
Is it due to human failings unaddressed,
Or the misalignment of yin and yang?
We now make this great vow,
To universally deliver all sentient beings.
Sweep away the obscuring clouds,
Reveal the great brightness of sun and moon.
Let the damp become dry,
Let the rotten flourish anew.
May seasons follow their course,
And peace be proclaimed.
*Qian*, origin, prosperity, benefit, perseverance.
Hasten as the statutes of the Lingji True Lords command.

**Prayer for Rain**
Drought demons rage,
Stones melt in the heat.
Crops wither in distress,
Anxious and trembling.
No god is left uninvoked,
Yet none descend.
Only Our True Lords,
Ascend to touch heaven’s heart.
Enacting heaven’s transformations,
Their vows are profound.
Warding off disasters, averting harm,
Closing yang, releasing yin.
Divine dragons manifest,
Bringing three days of rain.
With the august title *Lingji*,
To this very day.
Hasten as the statutes of the Lingji True Lords command.

**Incantation to Ward Off Pests and Protect Crops**
Heaven gives birth to the people,
Who depend on food.
The people toil,
Laboring in fields.
Why, O Heaven, inflict this scourge?
Self-reproach and remorse,
Hearts tremble with dread.
Only Our True Ones,
Whose virtue is cherishing life.
The Emperor’s wrath may be turned,
Heaven’s heart may be moved.
Spirits of the fields, attend,
We implore your care.
Banish the borers and cutworms,
And all their kind.
Spare our fields,
Let us sow and reap.
This year shall yield abundance,
Rich in grain and millet.
True Lords, True Lords,
Manifest in majesty.
Since you do not forsake us,
Attend to our duties.
Recite this divine incantation,
Hasten as the statutes command.

**Proclamation of the Golden Palace**
The Star of Literature fell to earth,
More than thirty years have passed.

**Vacancies in the Immortal Bureaus**
The offices of the Immortal Courts lie empty,
Their officials unappointed.
The selections of the Many Heavens proceed,
Yet none are found worthy.
According to the Primordial Yang Jade Calendar,
This duty belongs to the Three Dynasties.
We must seek those who have accumulated goodness and built merit,
Whom the Three Realms commend,
Whom the Five Emperors protect,
Whose names are recorded in the heavens,
To fill these posts.

The Radiant and Widespreadly Beneficent Perfected One of the Nine Heavens’ Golden Palace, Master of the Celestial Patterns Institute, shall act in accordance with his charge.
Xu Zhizheng’s writings are pure and sincere,
Renowned in his time.
Tested in both talent and virtue,
He is fit for the selection of Wenchang.
Heaven and humanity approve—
Do not persist in refusal.
In this ninth generation of the present age,
Whom but you shall we choose?
Our decree is just—
Go forth and strive with diligence.

You are hereby appointed as Chief Recorder of Wenchang,
With concurrent tenure of your former post.

**Proclamation of the Jade Palace**
The human form is hard to obtain,
Birth in the Central Land is rare.
We wish to unlock the mysteries of the Nine Heavens,
To succor the myriad people.
To propagate the Dao and spread its transformation,
To reverently uphold and enact it,
We must select Perfected Ones among the immortals
To fulfill this duty.

The Illustrious and Widespreadly Beneficent Perfected One of the Nine Heavens’ Jade Palace, Xu Zhie,
Has labored with earnest devotion,
Regarding the people as his children.
Long tested in external service,
His reputation and achievements are well-known.
Now, the Southern Dipper Bureau lacks its proper officer.

The office shall be filled by one capable, and in this, your ability is proven.
Let the aged find their proper end, the strong their proper use, the young their proper growth.
Let the widowed, orphaned, solitary, and childless all be provided for.
As for women with child—whether yet unborn or already delivered—let all be nurtured to life.
Let this be your mutual encouragement.

You are hereby specially appointed as Supreme Minister of the Southern Dipper’s Life-Recording Bureau, with concurrent tenure of your former post.

**Proclamation of the Jing Kingdom’s Immortal Consort**
The Immortal Consort of Benevolent Assistance and Kindness,
Extends benevolence to those below and embodies harmony in kindness.
With both virtues fully realized, this is the excellence of a noblewoman.
Thus, she aids the noble man without deviation or obstruction.
Her private concerns are set aside, her diligence unceasing day and night.
Within, she assists with compliance, as recorded in the rites.
A wife’s glory follows her husband’s honor.
She is hereby specially appointed as Immortal Consort, retaining her former name.

**Proclamation of the Wei Kingdom’s Immortal Consort**
The Immortal Consort of Virtuous Assistance and Grace,
Embodies compassion and grace, upholding the way of the wife.
She enables the lord of the land to accumulate merit and amass virtue,
Thus attaining rank and office—this is the power of her virtuous assistance.
Now, her illustrious rank is elevated, her esteemed title advanced.
She is hereby specially appointed as Immortal Consort, retaining her former name.

**Jade Palace’s Edict of Immortal Appointment**
Your bones and form align with immortality,
Long since inscribed upon the Crimson Terrace’s register.
As offices disperse and positions scatter,
Now, by the Jade Calendar’s selection, the time has come for your worthiness.
To manifest your goodness,
We hereby confer upon you the *Shangqing Dadong Secret Register*.

Minister Xu Zhizheng,
Devoted solely to the Dao, a disciple of Heaven,
His reputation and renown are well-established, his exemplary conduct enduring.
In poetry, he cherished the *Tangdi*, loving his younger brother and revering his elder.
In governance, he recited the *Er Tang*, his virtue residing in the people, his merit in the state.
Setting aside personal gain, he pondered rank and office—who could say it was undeserved?
Thus, he ascends to the title of Great Immortal of the Golden Palace,
And advances to the rank of Feathered Emolument of Wenchang.
Presiding over the literary balance, he inspires the scholar-gentry.
Mastering the subtle workings of Heaven and Earth, he ushers in the great peace of sun and moon.
His deeds fulfill the Three Thousand, his achievements extraordinary.
His office attains the first rank—how could we withhold this unparalleled honor?
Go forth, embody this new glory, and strengthen your former resolve.
He is hereby specially appointed as *Great Immortal of the Nine Heavens’ Golden Palace, Illuminating the Dao and Manifesting Virtue, Radiantly Spirited and Universally Beneficent Perfected One*,
Serving as Chief Recorder of Wenchang, with authority to sign documents for the Heavenly Mechanism Bureau.

**Jade Palace’s Edict of Immortal Appointment**
The Great Dao is impartial; sincerity takes form, and form becomes manifest.
The heavens select and order; let each hold office according to their ability.
With proven talent, no position shall remain vacant.
We hereby confer upon you the *Shangqing Dadong Secret Register*.

Minister Xu Zhie,
Guards the divine, takes goodness as his teacher,
Upholds the precepts, observes fasting, cultivates truth, and attains the Dao.
His hun-soul is the sun, his po-soul the moon,
Mastering the work of *li* and *kan*.
Timely rain and seasonable sunshine—externally, he embodies the transformations of Heaven and Earth.
Through labor, he stabilizes the state; his virtue resides in the people.
In bestowing rewards, why delay in extending grace?
Thus, he ascends to the title of Immortal of the Jade Palace,
And advances to the rank of Life-Recorder of the Southern Dipper.
People and creatures alike receive life and nurturance.
Governance and literature are administered with impartial rigor.
The people all declare it fitting—thus, this exceptional honor is added.
The noble man does not eat in idleness; he forever bears the responsibility of propagating the Dao.
In response to this glorious mandate, may you fulfill our deepest hopes.
He is hereby specially appointed as *Illustrious and Widespreadly Beneficent Perfected One of the Nine Heavens’ Jade Palace, Propagating Transformation and Upholding the Dao, Radiantly Spirited and Universally Beneficent Immortal*,
Provisionally serving as Minister of the Southern Dipper’s Life-Recording Bureau, with authority to sign documents for the Thunder and Mystery Bureau.

**Decree of Additional Rank and Title**
We observe that the twin gates of the Alchemical Palace stand grandly open,
And the silver seals of the two bureaus magnify the court’s mandate.
This further honor is bestowed, enhancing your radiance.
For titles and ranks must not be granted lightly,
Yet offices and emoluments serve to nurture virtue—let name match position.
Your ability is daily refined, ever centered in utmost sincerity.
From beginning to end, unwavering, neither boastful nor self-aggrandizing.
How splendid is your virtue, O minister!
Thus, these appointments are hereby confirmed, serving as the standard for such decrees.

**Decree of the Five Marshals’ Office**
We observe that one who excels as both general and minister embodies the fullness of civil and martial talent.
To bring fortune to the state and peace to the family relies solely on the power of the divine.
Moreover, his name is inscribed in the annals, his achievements engraved on the sacred bell.
Once he received the honor of posthumous titles; now, the fragrance of incense burns brightly.
Timely rain and sunshine harmonize in the villages, and all creatures dwell in tranquility.
In this tranquil peace, only by accumulating goodness and building merit can one unite hearts and assist in governance.
Above, he embodies the Illustrious and Radiant Virtue of the Perfected One;
Below, he extends the Universally Beneficent and Vastly Compassionate kindness of the Perfected One.
We shall test him in this—it is your strength.
Examine affairs with care, report fully and truthfully.
Review the old to understand the new, and receive this further title of honor.
For perpetual guidance, this decree is specially granted for your observance.
Uphold the precepts and aid the people.

On the third day of the third month in the year of Yi-Wei, Dingguang Bodhisattva, together with the Emperor of the Sacred Peaks, memorialized to grant Jiang Wang the title of **Nine Heavens Golden Portal Illuminated Dao Attaining Virtue Great Immortal Manifesting Numinous Universally Beneficent Perfected One**, charged with overseeing the Celestial Astronomy Bureau and acting with full authority. His consort, Lady Xu, was bestowed the title of **Assisting Benevolent and Kind Immortal Consort**.

Rao Wang was granted the title of **Nine Heavens Jade Portal Proclaiming Transformation Upholding Dao Supreme Immortal Radiant Numinous Universally Beneficent Perfected One**, charged with overseeing all bureaus of the Lower Earthly Prisons and acting with full authority, concurrently holding the provisional offices of **Southern Culmen Life-Registering Grand Minister and Thunderbolt Dark Mystery Affairs Commissioner**. His consort, Lady Tao, was bestowed the title of **Kindly Assisting Virtuous Immortal Consort**.

Further conferred was the celestial secret text, which states:
*The Three Departments and Eight Sceneries—only essence, qi, and spirit.*
*In stillness, refine breath; turn from dust to unite with the Real.*
*Avoid defilement; guard this secret text.*
*Study it to attain the Dao and ascend as a Perfected One; recite it to prolong life and extend destiny.*

On the third day of the third month, this is the day of my descent. Prepare a clean basin of pure water and place it upon a spotless table. Should one first develop sores or swellings, take this water, add a pinch of salt, burn incense, and recite the Perfected One’s numinous incantation seven times before applying it to the afflicted area. Observe abstinence for three days, and recovery will follow.

Henceforth, on the Three Origins, Eight Festivals, Gengshen, Jiazi days, and the birthdays of Buddhist sages, slaughter for blessings is forbidden; I shall not accept such offerings. Now appointed as **Heavenly Court Rectifying Governance Supreme Immortal**, you must reverently believe and practice accordingly.

**Matters of Virtuous Practice:**
1. **Revere Heaven and Earth.** Heaven covers and Earth bears—such is the work of transformation and nurturance.
2. **Trust in the Three Treasures.** Honor the Three Treasures; never slander them.
3. **Keep distance from ghosts and spirits.** Respect but remain distant; evil shall not disturb the upright.
4. **Remember ancestors.** The merits of ancestors and virtues of clans run deep.
5. **Be filial to parents.** Parents’ toil is boundless; their kindness is unmatched.
6. **Love siblings.** Brotherly kindness and fraternal respect are the love of limbs.
7. **Uphold righteousness with one’s spouse.** The way of husband and wife begins and ends in righteousness.
8. **Observe propriety with neighbors.** The classics say: when stepping out, act as if meeting a distinguished guest.
9. **Teach descendants.** Goodness is innate; through teaching, they become true persons.
10. **Diligently study poetry and books.** The books of sages and worthies, when read, reveal principle.
11. **Labor in farming and sericulture.** Agriculture and women’s work sustain life; diligence ensures clothing and food.
12. **Show kindness to birds and beasts.** All live and grow; never harbor thoughts of killing.
13. **Cultivate hidden virtue.** What is hidden virtue? It is nothing other than convenience and kindness.

*Record of the Immortal Xu, Scroll One* (End)
*Compiled by Fang Wenzhao of the Ming Dynasty. Five scrolls.*

**Record of the Immortal Xu, Scroll Two**
**Precepts of the Perfected Lords for Entering the Altar**

Upon entering the altar, each person shall take their place in order, preserve spirit and close the breath, knock the teeth nine times, swallow saliva nine times, and pace the void.

*The Supreme Ultimate divides high and deep,*
*Light and pure, it ascends to belong to Heaven.*
*If one cultivates the true Dao,*
*The body becomes a perfected immortal.*
*Deeds overflow the count of three thousand,*
*Time reaches forty thousand years.*
*The cinnabar terrace opens its treasure scrolls,*
*The golden mouth spreads its flowing transmission.*

**Prayer for Incense**
The censer burns with precious incense,
its smoke scattering through the jade heavens,
forming a cloud terrace,
adorned as the Dharma Realm.

Reverently, we burn the incense of the Dao, the incense of virtue, the incense of non-action, the pure incense of non-action, the naturally pure incense, the wondrous cavernous true incense, the numinous treasure bestowing incense, the incense transcending the Three Realms, and the true incense of the Three Luminaries. May it fill the jade halls of the Jasper Capital and pervade the Dharma Realm of the cosmos.

Today, we reverently burn this precious incense to offer in devotion to:
*The Great Immortal of the Golden Towers of the Nine Heavens, Illuminator of the Dao and Attainer of Virtue, Manifest Spirit of Universal Salvation, Pure and Subtle Cavernous Mystery, Void and Wondrous Responsive Compassionate Protector of the Nation and Shelterer of the People, Exalted Blessing and Vast Grace Perfected Lord;*
*The Supreme Immortal of the Jade Towers of the Nine Heavens, Proclaimer of Transformation and Upholder of the Teachings, Radiant Spirit of Vast Salvation, Lofty and Serene, Profound and Wondrous Responsive Benevolent Assistant to the Nation and Protector of the People, Abundant Blessing and Vast Grace Perfected Lord;*
*The Sacred Father, King Qi, Loyal and Martial Illustrious Perfected Lord;*
*The Sacred Mother, Lady Tian, Benevolent and Longevous Virtuous Immortal Consort;*
*The Sacred Elder Brothers, King Tang, King Hong, King E, and King Guangling;*
*The Sacred Uncles, Duke of the Nation’s Protection and Duke of the Nation’s Service;*
*The Sacred Sons-in-Law, Marquis of Martial Peace and Marquis of Tranquil Nation;*
*The Sacred Sons, Marquis of Preserving Greatness, Marquis of Manifesting Trust, Marquis of Preserving Trust, Marquis of Preserving Peace, and Marquis of Martial Peace;*
*The Sacred Nephews, Marquis of Illustrious Virtue, Marquis of Peaceful Stability, and Marquis of Supreme Peace;*
*The Sacred Grandsons, Marquis of Martial Prosperity and Marquis of Southern Prosperity;*
*All the noble lords and ministers;*
*The Heavenly Mechanism Bureau of the Great Cavern Scriptures and Registers, the Heavenly Pivot Bureau, the Thunder Department’s Celestial Patterns Bureau, the Heavenly Records Bureau;*
*All the officials and generals of the Earthly Prisons who carry out decrees, drive away evil, seize malevolent spirits, transmit talismans, and command the Dharma;*
*Those who dispel disasters, deliver from calamities, expel misfortune, and ward off monstrosities;*
*The altar-monitoring and Dharma-protecting generals;*
*The inspecting and patrolling generals;*
*The Venerable Spirit of the Year Star;*
*The twelve monthly generals and disciples;*
*The star officials of one’s original destiny and life-spirit;*
*The immortals of the Wind and Thunder Departments;*
*The Left and Right Chief Ministers and Grand Stewards;*
*The ministers of the Six Ministries and the inner court nobles;*
*The Left and Right Supreme Stewards of Life-Recording and Longevity-Recording;*
*The Left and Right Supreme Stewards of the Bureau of Records and the Bureau of Blessings;*
*The Left and Right Attendants and Envoys;*
*The officials and subordinates of the Hundred Offices and various bureaus;*
*All the noble lords and ministers;*
*The officials of the twenty-four bureaus under the Left and Right Bureaus of Blessings;*
*The Left and Right Guiding Immortal Officials;*
*The Perfected Immortals of the Three Heavenly Cowrie Towers, Cultivators of Benevolence and Nurturers of Rectitude;*
*The True Persons of Spreading Numinous Power and Vast Salvation;*
*The Venerable King of Numinous Might and Clear Rivers;*
*The Marshal Yuan of Eternal Peace and the Guardian of the Capital;*
*The Marshal Yuan of Martial Peace and the Guardian of the Frontier;*
*The Marshal Wei, Left Supervisor of the Gate of Discipline;*
*The Marshal Zhao, Right Supervisor of the Gate of Discipline and Commander of the United Armies;*
*The Marshal Diao, Commander of the Vanguard;*
*All their valiant soldiers and fierce warriors;*
*The Left and Right Marshals Yue and Xu;*
*The attendants of the Left and Right Traveling Palaces;*
*The officials of the Bureaus of Records, Merit, Personnel, and Documents;*
*The officials of the Bureaus of Agriculture, Crops, Silk, and Hemp;*
*The officials of the Bureaus of Markets, Commerce, Crafts, and Materials;*
*The kitchen officials, entertainment officials, and musicians;*
*The celestial, divine, and human swift messengers;*
*The officials of divination, lots, cups, and phoenixes;*
*The dream-transmitting youths;*
*The spirit bureau officers;*
*The attendants of the hall and talisman;*
*The incense officials;*
*The envoys and various immortals;*
*The donors and patrons of the altar;*
*The virtuous and renowned;*
*The local earth gods of this palace;*
*The deities of all villages and temples;*
*The disciples of kings and marquises.*

May each person’s worshipped deities, the united numinous powers of the Lingji Palace, and the entire assembly of sacred presences rely upon this true incense in universal offering.

This incense is the scattered radiance of jade blossoms,
the purple qi congealing into smoke,
a fragrant cloud woven densely,
directly filling the Nine Heavens.

May it be that the golden lads attend the incense,
the jade maidens transmit words and scatter flowers,
ascending to the presence of the true ones.
Whatever is petitioned and whatever is wished,
may all be granted as spoken.
*May it enter the mind.*

Today, as we open the altar and make this declaration, we humbly pray that the true compassion may deign to bestow its luminous regard.
We bow our heads and take refuge in the Boundless Great Dao.

**Chanting the Dao**
All in the Daoist ritual assembly,
each directs their mind to take refuge in the Two and the One,
reciting all the blossoming hymns of the Central Land.
*Three circumambulations.*

**Purifying the Altar**
The utmost true is only pure;
how can it descend to defiled realms?
When the dusty world is not yet cleansed,
how can the mysterious and primordial be manifested?
It is necessary to sprinkle the Dharma water from a single branch,
instantly dispelling the demonic miasma for ten thousand miles.
The nine phoenixes soar, spitting flames to break impurity.
The five dragons surge, descending true qi to expel evil.
May all who take refuge attain response in full.

The supreme and mysterious words of the Most High shall now be reverently recited.
*Within the cavernous void, the clouds...*

*The Heavenly Worthy Who Subdues Demons and Shields from Impurity paces the void:*
The five marshals proceed to the marshal’s presence to offer incense...

We humbly submit:
To transform on a grand scale is called sageliness.
That which is sagely yet unknowable is called spirit.

The Most Sagely abides in non-action,
naturally responding with emptiness.
Revering the spirits as if present,
all that is felt is wholly communicated.
Since what is held in mind is thus,
know that their mirroring is not far.

We humbly invoke the Five Great Marshals—Zha, Bian, Wei, Zhao, and Diao—
whose rank surpasses the five marshals,
whose valor leads the three armies.
They dance with shields and feathers between the two steps,
wielding the great axe of authority.
As generals they march forth, as ministers they return,
mastering both civil and martial arts.
They aid the state and pacify the people,
bearing the trust of ruler and subjects alike.
Majestic within the palace, solemn within the temple,
their fame resounds, their numinous power shines.
Too wondrous for words, they conceal their wrath.
All are extraordinary men of Yan and Zhao,
befriending one another like Lian and Lan.
In unity and harmony, they are trusted and employed.
They scale mountains and sail seas,
coming from a thousand miles away without hesitation.
They ride mists and soar through the void,
ascending directly to the heights of the Nine Heavens.

Today, as we perform this rite of requital and prayer for blessings,
the altar is purified, and the liturgy is about to commence.
We bow our heads in sincerity, wholeheartedly turning to the Dao.
To invite the true presence of the deities,
we must humbly reveal our innermost devotion,
relying on the Five Marshals to convey our plea.
We reverently beseech the Most High to descend,
greatly bestowing their compassionate vow.
May they grant our supplication,
and we offer our devout worship.

*All rise, each with reverence*
*Incense is offered*

With focused mind, the first offering of incense:
May the fragrance reach the Lingji Palace,
pervading the Lingji Palace,
where the sacred realm forms a canopy of clouds.
We offer to the Sacred Father, Prince Qi,
the Loyal and Martial Illustrious True Lord.

With focused mind, the second offering of incense:
May the fragrance reach the Lingji Palace,
pervading the Lingji Palace,
where the true realm forms a canopy of treasures.
We offer to the Great Immortal of the Golden Towers of the Nine Heavens,
Manifesting Dao and Attaining Virtue,
Universally Revealing Numinous Aid,
Pure and Subtle Cavernous Void,
Mysteriously Responsive,
Compassionate and Benevolent,
Protecting the State and Sheltering the People,
Bestowing Blessings and Vast Grace,
True Lord Hong’en.

With focused mind, the third offering of incense:
May the fragrance reach the Lingji Palace,
pervading the Lingji Palace,
where the immortal realm forms a canopy of flowers.
We offer to the Supreme Immortal of the Jade Towers of the Nine Heavens,
Proclaiming Transformation and Upholding the Dao,
Illustrious and Universally Aiding,
Lofty and Profound,
Serene and Mysterious,
Wondrously Responsive,
Benevolent and Compassionate,
Assisting the State and Protecting the People,
Bestowing Blessings and Vast Grace,
True Lord Hong’en.

Kneeling before the censer:
The Dao is studied in the heart,
the heart transmits through incense.
Holding the jade censer,
the mind abides in the Nine Heavens.
May the True Lords deign to look down,
their immortal pendants approaching the hall.
Let our petition be conveyed,
directly reaching the Nine Heavens.

*All pay homage to the Perfected Ones, visualizing as prescribed*

**Five Stars Mantra**
The Five Stars array their radiance,
illuminating the five directions.
The Water Star averts disaster,
the Power of Wood brings prosperity.
Mars dispels misfortune,
Venus repels warfare.
Saturn guards the four quarters,
bringing benefit to family and state.
Inscribed on jade tablets,
recorded in the celestial chambers.
Riding the whirlwind and spreading light,
they soar through the great void.
Emerging from and entering the unseen,
they wander and feast in the ten directions.
Five-colored clouds form their canopy,
summoning spirits and commanding winds.
They employ the myriad numina,
harmonizing: "Above, protect the Immortal Elders."

*Twenty-four strikes of the Dharma drum resound*

**Opening the Censer**
The Most High Lord of the Five Numinous Ones summons forth
the Three and Five within our bodies,
the Merit Officers to left and right,
the Incense Officials and Envoys,
the Golden Lads who attend the incense,
the Jade Maidens who transmit words and scatter flowers,
the Daily Incense Officials,
the Merit Officer Envoys,
the Three Qi True Spirits—
hasten to ascend and convey this petition!

To the Five Great Marshals—Zha, Bian, Wei, Zhao, and Diao—
the Two Marshals of Yue and Xu,
the Heavenly Ding and Valiant Soldiers,
the Divine Officials to left and right:
We now ascend the altar for this Dharma rite,
reverently performing this requital and prayer for blessings.
All our sincere entreaties are set forth in the written petition.
Through this rite,
may we receive the vital qi of the true and authentic,
flowing into our bodies,
so that our words of supplication
swiftly reach the Most High Three Treasures,
the Heavenly Lords,
the Great Immortal of the Golden Towers of the Nine Heavens,
Manifesting Dao and Attaining Virtue,
Universally Revealing Numinous Aid,
Pure and Subtle Cavernous Void,
Mysteriously Responsive,
Compassionate and Benevolent,
Protecting the State and Sheltering the People,
Bestowing Blessings and Vast Grace,
True Lord Hong’en,
and the Supreme Immortal of the Jade Towers of the Nine Heavens,
Proclaiming Transformation and Upholding the Dao,
Illustrious and Universally Aiding,
Lofty and Profound,
Serene and Mysterious,
Wondrously Responsive,
Benevolent and Compassionate,
Assisting the State and Protecting the People,
Bestowing Blessings and Vast Grace,
True Lord Hong’en.

Before the Sacred Ones, we bow once.

We, the undersigned [Name], together with the altar officials and assembly,
jointly and sincerely petition the Nine Heavens’ Golden Towers.
The sacred titles remain as above.

We humbly reflect:
Gou Long governs earth, pillars sustain valleys,
thus the altars of state and grain are established.
The Zhou revered scent, the Shang revered sound,
to commune with the power of the divine.
Not that blood sacrifices alone suffice,
for even humble offerings may be presented to kings and lords.
That which is sagely yet unknowable is called spirit.
That which is spirit yet can be named enters into sageliness.

We reverently invoke
the Great Immortal of the Golden Towers of the Nine Heavens,
Manifesting Dao and Attaining Virtue,
Universally Revealing Numinous Aid,
Pure and Subtle Cavernous Void,
Mysteriously Responsive,
Compassionate and Benevolent,
Protecting the State and Sheltering the People,
Bestowing Blessings and Vast Grace,
True Lord Hong’en,
and the Supreme Immortal of the Jade Towers of the Nine Heavens,
Proclaiming Transformation and Upholding the Dao,
Illustrious and Universally Aiding,
Lofty and Profound,
Serene and Mysterious,
Wondrously Responsive,
Benevolent and Compassionate,
Assisting the State and Protecting the People,
Bestowing Blessings and Vast Grace,
True Lord Hong’en.

Uprightness is their virtue,
moving people with fortune and misfortune.
Hidden in earth, they are earth;
hidden in heaven, they are heaven—
their numinous power is unfathomable.
When they command the sun, it shines;
when they command the rain, it falls—
solely wielding the power of creation.
Their fame resounds, their presence overflows.
Above, they assist the Dipper Perfected at the North Pole,
silently participating in the mysterious learning of the Eastern Flower.
In union with the Dao, they guard the divine.
Their names are inscribed in the Golden Towers,
honored with titles of three or four characters.
Their offices shine in the treasure palace,
fitting the three thousand ranks of conduct.
Responding to circumstances, they vow to deliver people.
Having received the grace of their sheltering care,
how dare we neglect the rites of prayer and exorcism?

Reverently, as the divine carriage descends to the altar,
some wear immortal pendants, their steps measured,
eight phoenixes singing behind.
Some don court robes, their presence majestic,
a hundred riders welcoming before and after.
The immortal retinue arrays in splendor,
divine officials guarding left and right.
We welcome the True Ones with humble offerings,
their virtuous mirror perceiving our sincerity.
Unworthy as we are, we bow our heads again and again,
reverently inviting the divine presence.

**Inviting the Sacred Ones**
We respectfully invoke.

The Most Radiant and Dao-Attaining, Virtue-Manifesting Great Immortal of the Nine Heavens’ Golden Portal, whose boundless efficacy pervades the Pure Subtlety of the Cavernous Mystery, whose subtle responsiveness is vast and empty, whose compassion and kindness protect the state and shelter the people, whose abundant blessings bestow vast grace—Perfected Lord of Majestic Favor,

The Most Illustrious and Teaching-Spreading, Dao-Propagating Supreme Immortal of the Nine Heavens’ Jade Portal, whose luminous efficacy is far-reaching and all-embracing, whose lofty clarity and profound tranquility subtly respond with benevolence, whose aid to the state and protection of the people bring exalted blessings and vast grace—Perfected Lord of Majestic Favor.

The sacred ranks remain as before.
We humbly beseech Your True Compassion to descend upon this altar.
Having already received Your gracious descent in response to our invocation,
we now invite the immortal assembly to take their ordered seats in due rank.

The Jiao officiants reverently bow in devotion,
present incense,
offer the first libation of wine,
and scatter blossoms.

We, [Name], in shared sincerity, reverently address the sacred ranks as before.

We have heard that renown in benevolence and righteousness
traces its lineage to the scions of kings.
Unbending loyalty and martial valor
inherited the noble ranks of the State of Qi.
Benevolent fame first flourished in Min,
while virtuous repute spread far across land and sea.
Names were inscribed on bronze tripods,
and deeds recorded in historical annals.
Stationed south of the Gorges, the people remained undisturbed.
Raising banners on Aofeng, the remnants of bandits were eradicated.
Thus, the blessed land was secured,
and all equally enjoyed the gifts of a Yao-like reign.
How could one forget such grace, even to repay with withered grass?
The ode to the sweet pear tree still resounds.
In death, temples and sacrifices;
in life, enfeoffment—
this is the utmost honor.
Teaching the Dao to the people,
laboring to pacify the state—
to this day, these are praised.

Of old, even grasses and trees responded to the mountain’s numen.
Now, fields are spared the scourge of floods.
Boats striking rocks heard the cry of the Yellow Banner’s rescue.
Neighboring fires turned back with the wind,
forever sparing the threat of scorched chimneys.
In Jiading, locusts did not cross the border;
in Baoqing, drought demons wrought no disaster.
When the red serpent appeared, rain poured forth;
when the Nine Heavens’ divine dragon emerged, thunder roared.
For ten thousand li, no trace was seen—
yet how did the night reveal celestial lamps?
No sound was heard—
yet how did the day resound with strings and woodwinds?
Deeds endured for a thousand years, carved in stone;
enfeoffments through successive generations, inscribed in gold.
Thus, scholars and commoners journeyed from afar to pay homage,
and incense and offerings were reverently presented through all seasons.

Only virtue is upheld—
not merely the fragrance of millet and grain.
Only the proper kind is venerated—
especially the purity of sacrificial offerings.
Building merit and accumulating goodness,
holding precepts and practicing purification.
Had this not ascended to the heart of Heaven,
how could one have transcended to the ranks of immortals?

By imperial decree,
we revere the mysterious wind,
inscribing the names of the Golden and Jade Portals,
bestowing the titles of Great Immortal and Supreme Perfected.
The Dao is our Dao,
virtue is our virtue.
Transforming the teachings of gods and spirits,
the divine teachings do not merely glorify a single moment or a single person—
they illuminate what came before
and inspire what comes after.
Teaching harmony among kin,
the Hall of Joyful Feasting stands.
Above, we gaze upon the august majesty of the Sacred Father and Sacred Mother;
below, the Sacred Sons and Sacred Grandsons enjoy prosperity.
The Sacred Uncle’s name is recorded in the Purple Palace;
the Sacred Elder Brother receives temple sacrifices in Jinling.
The Divine Empress and Lady,
solely in charge of the Register of Births.
The Sacred Consort and Immortal [Title],
surrounded by the ranks of inner attendants.
Some oversee the Bureau of Blessings,
others hold the offices of ministers and nobles.
Authority surpasses the Five Marshals,
valor leads the Three Armies.
Whether martial or civil,
whether left or right.
The temple guards the land of the Seven Min—
its grandeur unmatched in virtue.
Its numen rivals the Five Peaks—
who but the Most Sacred could compare?
Merits towering, name enduring,
virtue extending to all beings.
By the shelter of the divine,
we are left in peace.
Every sip and bite—
dare we ever forget?
Thrice bathed, thrice perfumed—
we revere as if You were present.

Now, as we welcome Your precious carriage,
deign to regard this humble servant.
The diligence of the purification rites
has gathered the feathered ones;
we dare present the auspicious "Empty Song of the Azure Heavens."

We, your servants, bow a hundred times,
reverently wishing the present Emperor
ten thousand years of life as father and mother of the realm,
safeguarding descendants with security,
bestowing upon the sovereign a thousand blessings and a hundred fortunes.
May the imperial enterprise endure forever.

All memorial texts have been duly recited.
The memorial is now proclaimed.
As the text has been fully declaimed,
we humbly beseech the immortal compassion to deign to peruse it.

Averting calamities and warding off disasters,
the rites are especially solemn in the sacrificial canon.
Repaying merit and exalting virtue,
it is fitting to advance the immortal ranks.
May they be recommended for the vermilion records of the Golden Portal,
honored to attend the incense table of the Jade Emperor.
Inhaling and exhaling the Two Qi,
profoundly mastering the methods of emerging from the blue and entering the mysterious.
The Seven Fluids circulating,
attaining the subtleties of embracing the yellow and returning to the purple.
In oneself, the beauty of self-cultivation;
toward others, the merit of universal salvation.
All that is felt is surely communicated;
all that is sought is surely answered.
Relieving the people’s suffering—
what need is there for Bian Que’s prescriptions?
Divining the yin and yang of land—
silently imparting the learning of Guo Pu.
For those seeking marriage—
harmony in family and household.
For those desiring heirs—
the birth of sons and grandsons.
For those pursuing office—
exhorted to diligence and filial piety.
For those establishing themselves or engaging in trade—
taught that benevolence and righteousness are profit.
Farmers toil in the fields;
artisans refine their skills.
The distant are pleased and the near come forth,
treasuring benevolence and manifesting its use.
Turning their hearts toward the Dao,
all receive the grace of enlightenment.
From white-haired elders to children with hanging locks,
all rely on Your sheltering care.

Today, we conduct this rite of gratitude and prayer for blessings.
Again, we offer fragrant incense,
welcoming the descent of the True Ones.
Once more, we present the pure libation,
praying for the arrival of the divine carriage.

We humbly pray:
The Most Radiant and Dao-Attaining, Virtue-Manifesting Great Immortal of the Nine Heavens’ Golden Portal, whose boundless efficacy pervades the Pure Subtlety of the Cavernous Mystery, whose subtle responsiveness is vast and empty, whose compassion and kindness protect the state and shelter the people, whose abundant blessings bestow vast grace—Perfected Lord of Majestic Favor,

The Most Illustrious and Teaching-Spreading, Dao-Propagating Supreme Immortal of the Nine Heavens’ Jade Portal, whose luminous efficacy is far-reaching and all-embracing, whose lofty clarity and profound tranquility subtly respond with benevolence, whose aid to the state and protection of the people bring exalted blessings and vast grace—Perfected Lord of Majestic Favor.

May the Register of Blessings come,
bestowing boundless feasts for eternal enjoyment.
May the land of Hua-Xia be purified,
supporting the imperial enterprise forever.

Reverently bowing in devotion,
presenting incense,
offering the second libation of wine,
and scattering blossoms.

We, [Name], together with the altar officials and all present,
in shared sincerity, reverently address the sacred ranks as before.

We have heard that the Luo Pond Stele,
through all ages, cannot efface its heroic spirit.

The Thousand-Year Grotto of Eastern Florescence—who has inherited its true wind to this day? Solemnly we recall the earth-guarding deities, whose deeds have amassed boundless merit. Their skeletal forms merge with immortals in vast beneficence, their literary brilliance rivals that of Lord Liu. If not celestial essences stored in the stars, they must be the finest nurtured by mountains and rivers. Their poems, songs, and odes endure in recitation, demanding solemn inscription—inscribed once, inscribed again, inscribed repeatedly. Their words on fortune and misfortune, blessings and calamities, never err. Yet we dare not presume: first we invoke, then invoke again, and humbly beseech a third invocation. The principles of manifest and hidden are revealed with clarity; the mechanisms of rise and fall are foreseen. Their countenance is grave and majestic—feared like the biting frost and scorching sun. Their Dao is lofty and far-reaching—revered like the Northern Dipper and Mount Tai. Their virtue shines resplendently; their divine efficacy gleams sharply.

Today, we establish this ritual altar to requite kindness and pray for blessings. May we humbly beseech: the Three Luminaries remain balanced, cold and heat arrive in season; the Five Grains ripen, and the people flourish. May all things be free from pestilence, and the state abound in auspicious omens. All that is created and sustained shall return to the Great Dao.

Reverently bowing in devotion,
presenting incense,
offering the final libation of wine.
Scattering blossoms, chanting scriptures, and proclaiming the memorial.

Entering the Seven Governors’ Lamps to fulfill vows and offer profound gratitude.

We, [Name], together with the altar officials and all present,
once more kindle incense of renown,
universally offering reverence.
The sacred ranks as before.

We have heard that the towering peaks of Ao rise so high they may grasp the stars of heaven. The dragon’s head rears proudly, bestowing abundant rain and dew upon the mortal realm. Having long received their grace in ordinary days, how shall we repay them in this moment? Pure offerings are laid forth, though we are shamed by the lack of jade urns and golden nectar. The immortals’ fare consists of nothing but fiery jujubes and intertwined pears. Now the precious talismanic incense has burned low, the silver lamp’s flame grows cold. Star-crowned and feather-robed, the steps of the void resound far into the Jade Palace. Cloud chariots and mist-borne carriages, the procession prepares to return to the Golden Portal. Though our hearts race with longing, we earnestly pray for blessings ever more abundant.

Thus it is spoken.

Recite the Ten Contemplations:
First, body and mind grow pure and cool.
Second, the nature’s wisdom becomes perfectly luminous.
Third, the Dao is revered and virtue exalted.
Fourth, conduct is fulfilled and merit accomplished.
Fifth, the hun-soul and spirit become serene and upright.
Sixth, demon kings offer protection and welcome.
Seventh, celestial officials bestow blessings.
Eighth, the underworld erases one’s name.
Ninth, the dark paths do not approach.
Tenth, the Pure Land grants eternal life.

Replenish the incense burner.
May the Incense Officials and Envoys, the Divine Lords of the Left and Right, and the Attendant Spirit-Officials of the Incense,
cause this place of our ritual to naturally birth golden elixir, cinnabar, and azure mushrooms.
May the assembled hosts of a hundred spirits and perfected beings rejoice in this gathering before the incense burner.
May the jade maidens and immortal youths of the ten directions receive the rising incense smoke,
and swiftly convey the words we have just uttered,
directly to the *Perfected of the Utmost Non-Polar Great Dao, Radiant Dao and Penetrating Virtue, Great Immortal Manifesting Universal Salvation, Pure and Subtle Cavern-Mystery, Void and Wondrous Response, Compassionate and Benevolent Protector of the Nation and Shelter of the People, August Spirit of Vast Grace and Great Favor, Perfected Lord*;
and to the *Perfected of the Jade Towers of the Nine Heavens, Propagating Transformation and Upholding the Dao, Supreme Immortal of Illustrious Efficacy and Vast Salvation, Lofty and Profound, Vast and Tranquil, Subtle and Responsive, Benevolent and Kind, Assistant of the Nation and Protector of the People, Exalted Spirit of Abundant Blessings and Great Favor, Perfected Lord*.

Escort forth the *Holy Father, Loyal and Martial Supporter of the Luminous*.

Upon the completion of the ritual fast, we reverently bear the profound grace. With devoted hearts and bowed heads, we now send forth the *Perfected Lords of Vast Grace of the Golden Towers of the Nine Heavens* and the *Perfected Lords of Vast Grace of the Jade Towers of the Nine Heavens*. The cloud-borne chariots do not tarry, nor can the crane-drawn carriages be detained. When future rites are held, we shall once more extend our invitation.

**Returning Chant**
The paired chariots return, borne on five-colored clouds,
Soaring high into the ninefold heavens.
Swiftly they vanish into the distant skies,
While the ritual site abounds with fragrant qi.
Profound grace suffuses the cosmos,
Blessings and fortune fill mountains and rivers.
Longing for the path of immortals,
Freely they ascend to the Great Loftiness.

Holy virtue endures in the ritual teachings,
The fast bestows long life and prosperity.
Life is prolonged by the jade tablets,
Petitions are presented in golden missives.
Sins are erased from the Northern Bureau,
Names are inscribed in the Southern Prosperity.
All the living enjoy extended years,
While the Perfected descend with auspicious blessings.

For the merits of the rites just performed, we pray the Perfected Lords bestow flowing grace and favor. Together, may all rely on virtuous deeds to ascend the Way, and may all devotees receive this offering.

**Dedication**
The Great Dao knows no bounds,
Like the radiance of good companions in the light.
The Perfect City responds to sincerity,
As echoes answer within the valley.
Now, for so-and-so, we humbly pray:
May the one who dwells in the northern palace’s splendor
Enjoy rivers clear and seas calm.
May their longevity match the steadfastness of the southern mountains,
With earth enduring and heaven eternal.
May civil and martial officials alike
See their ranks and emoluments increase.
May all within the palace gates
Rely on health and peace.
May the realm delight in the winds of great peace,
And all beings benefit from the power of nurturing virtue.

Relying on the assembly of the Dharma, we offer this for the highest good.

Recitation:
The Three Pure Ones and Three Realms Heavenly Worthies,
The Nine Heavens’ Blessing Heavenly Worthies,
The Ten Directions’ Numinous Treasure Heavenly Worthies,
Whose merits are beyond conception.

The Perfected Lords’ ritual is complete.
The Perfected Lords’ vows are fulfilled.

**Incense Offering**

Today, with reverence, we kindle precious incense,
devoutly offering it to the **Nine Heavens’ Golden Palace Illuminated Dao, Virtue-Attaining Great Immortal, Manifestly Numinous, Universally Salvific, Pure and Subtle, Vast and Void, Wondrously Responsive, Compassionate and Benevolent, Protector of the Realm, Shelter of the People, Exalted in Blessing, Vast in Grace Perfected Lord**;
to the **Nine Heavens’ Jade Palace Proclaiming Transformation, Upholding the Dao, Supreme Immortal, Radiantly Numinous, Vastly Salvific, Lofty and Bright, Vast and Serene, Profoundly Tranquil, Wondrously Responsive, Benevolent and Kind, Assisting the Realm, Blessing the People, Abundant in Blessing, Vast in Grace Perfected Lord**;
and to the **Palace Immortals and all Divine Officials**, universally offered together.

We have heard that the manifest virtue of the gods
is called uprightness and called wisdom.
What mortals commonly desire
is ease and wealth, honor and nobility.
Sacrifice must bring blessing—
neither too spare in ritual nor too lavish.
For four hundred years, temple offerings have flourished,
incense fires burning ever bright.
Steles bear a thousand characters,
inscriptions to be heard and known.
Their luminous, undying names,
their awe-inspiring, life-like righteousness—
merits securing the altars of state,
virtues abiding in all living beings.
Farmers toil in the fields,
reaping the bounty of millet, rice, and grain.
Artisans hone their crafts,
meeting the standards of plumb, line, compass, and square.
Scholars establish themselves through loyalty and filial piety,
merchants profit through benevolence and righteousness.
Those who seek marriage
find harmony in home and household.
Those who pray for descendants
beget sons and grandsons.
Wind to the people, rain to the people—
all fulfill the wishes of growth and nurture.
Clothing for me, food for me—
all partake in the kindness of warmth and sustenance.
Bestowed upon the myriad things, all is fitting;
ordained through the four seasons, all is in order.
Gazing up to them is like beholding Mount Tai or the Northern Dipper—
their radiance is vast, never distant from us.
When they manifest, they appear as auspicious stars and felicitous clouds,
and all vie to behold them, counting it their joy.

We now offer grand rites to proclaim their numinosity.
Once they received the honor of imperial bestowal,
now they bear the favor of Heaven’s grace.
Their rank ascends to Golden Palace and Jade Palace,
their names advance to Great Immortal and Supreme Immortal.
Their honorific titles are exalted,
their majesty resplendent.
Their sacrifices endure for a hundred generations,
their standards guide the myriad spirits.
They stand as elders among the great creators,
ancient yet never aging.

We, though our hearts yearn for the Dao,
are unworthy in talent.
We humbly express our private gratitude,
offering this meager token of reverence.
With solemn assembly prepared,
we venture to disturb the gods’ wisdom.

We pray:
May jade phoenixes sing *jiu-jiu*,
may eight dragons coil in winding flight.
Lead the clouds and rainbows to descend,
command the gates of Heaven to swing wide.
First send Feng Jiang as vanguard,
then dispatch Fei Lian to follow in haste.
Bestow your grace with ease,
grant us the serene light of longevity.
Pour cassia wine and peppered ale,
steam orchid-wrapped delicacies on fragrant mats.
Roam freely, linger in leisure,
turn back in fond remembrance.

Our humble hearts are filled with earnest devotion,
awaiting your manifest presence.
All the Perfected Lords’ original vows and divine incantations,
we now diligently recite—
**Perfected Lords, Perfected Lords, Northern Dipper Great Spirits...**

The preceding divine incantations have been fully proclaimed.
We now reverently invite:
**Sacred Father, Loyal and Martial Duke of Qi, Illuminating and Upholding Perfected Lord**;
**Sacred Mother, Benevolent and Longevous, Kind and Virtuous Immortal Consort**;
the **Two Perfected Lords of the Nine Heavens’ Golden Palace and Jade Palace**;
the **Two Immortal Consorts of Jing and Wei Kingdoms**.
May their divine processions descend to join the assembly,
where the host of Perfected Ones array themselves in ranks to pay homage.

The homage complete, each ascends to their ritual seat.
With devotion, we bow and offer incense.

**Chanting Incense, Holding the Censer**
We humbly submit:
Bright virtue is offered, yet not through millet or grain can its fragrance be matched.
Those who walk the path of goodness
share their scent with orchids and angelica.
This incense—
jade censers emit auspiciousness,
golden tripods present omens.
Thick and billowing,
it coalesces into clouds and mist.
Warm and misty,
it nurtures the spring of the cosmos.
Holding it, messengers stand before us;
attending it, youths stand behind us.

If this is a ritual feast:
We bow our heads in reverence, devoutly offering.
If not:
The first libation of wine is presented.

With this, we accompany the sacred assembly,
directing our hearts in sincere offering.

**Incense Verse**
Cloud lotuses grow in Heaven,
strong winds scatter them across the four seas.
Deep within the dragon palace’s secrets,
sea gods present them to the immortals.
Today, with fervent devotion,
the fragrant smoke ascends to the purple court.
Penetrating and attaining the effortless,
all prayers are fulfilled as wished.

**Response:**
All together, with one heart, we offer.

**Scattering Flowers.**
The censer’s smoke rises in swirling eddies.
Circling the altar.

**Chanting Water, Holding the Water Vessel**

Prostrate, we reflect:
Even the sweat of toil may be offered to lords and nobles,
for loyalty and trust alone form its essence.
Yet the source-water flows ceaselessly day and night,
and we humbly confess our voices exceed our merit.

This water—
neither turbid nor dim—
remains ever clear, ever pure.
In Heaven, it becomes rain and dew,
caught by bronze pillars and golden stalks.
On Earth, it is sweet spring,
consumed like jade nectar and liquid jasper.
The wise act where nothing is lacking,
serving the highest good without contention.
No water fails to flow east—
its source arises here.

If this is a ritual feast:
We bow our heads in reverence, devoutly offering.
If not:
The second libation of wine is presented.
With this, we accompany the sacred assembly,
directing our hearts in sincere offering.

**Water Verse**
The silver river of Heaven overflows,
its limpid depths reflecting the ten directions.
Transformed, it descends as rain and dew,
bestowing boundless grace upon Heaven and Earth.
Moistening below, it revives the withered;
permeating, it nourishes all life.
Pouring this water, we express our red hearts—
body and mind wholly cleansed.

**Response:**
All together, with one heart, we offer.

**Scattering Flowers.**
Not from earthly veins, the flowing source—
scattering blossoms in the grove.
Irrigation from the celestial river.
*[Chanting continues.]*
Circling afar.

**Praise of Flowers / Offering of Flowers**
We bow in reverence, observing how layer upon layer of jade-green leaves
provide sheltering shade for the threads of purity.
How lush and fragrant the jasper blossoms,
born in the courtyard of the Great Possession.
These flowers—
their fragrance arises from □,
their hues know no fixed form.
The red lotus of the pond
suddenly shifts to emerald.
The white peony
may be dyed to gold.
From the Palace of Broad Cold, a single osmanthus branch—
its shadow cast upon the autumn moon.
Within the Wu-ling grotto, a thousand peach trees—
their dimpled smiles in the spring breeze.
To pour forth the devotion of sunflowers,
we humbly present the rites of duckweed and white milfoil.

If this is a ritual feast:
We bow our heads in reverence, devoutly offering.
If not:
The final libation of wine is presented.
With this, we accompany the sacred assembly,
directing our hearts in sincere offering.

**Flower Verse**
Rare blossoms flourish in the Dark Garden,
their roots spreading through the ten directions.
Standing tall for eight hundred years,
their fragrance descends to the dusty world.
Resplendent in the realm of radiant light,
scattering like jeweled flowers in the rain.
Gathering the purest essence,
we now offer them together.

**Response:**
All together, with one heart, we offer.

**Scattering Flowers.**
Where do the scattered flowers find their fragrance?

Circling in procession, we recite the *Scripture of the Perfected Lords*, having heard its teachings.
Thus we submit: when the spirit wanders in the Dao, sight perceives nothing, hearing discerns nothing.
When the spirit abides in the Dao, what was before the eyes suddenly appears behind.
Hidden yet never ceasing to be hidden—its name arises from a forced designation.

Since the dawn of the Crimson Clarity and the unfolding of heaven’s charts, the descent of celestial scriptures began.
When the Celestial Scribe wielded the brush, the flourishing of human culture arose.
The Emperor’s Renown bestowed it before the Terrace of Pastoral Virtue;
the Yellow Emperor transmitted it upon Mount Emei.
Some received it at Gourd Valley, fulfilling the vow of Helü’s sealed talismans.
Some descended upon Bell Mountain, accomplishing the merit of Great Yu.
How much more does the transmission of these scriptural teachings
awaken the understanding of all sentient beings?

This is solely by the grace of
