**The Perfected Lord of the Nine Heavens’ Golden Portal, Illuminator of the Dao and Attainer of Virtue, Great Immortal Manifesting Numinous Pervasive Salvation, Pure and Subtle Cavernous Mystery, Void and Wondrous Response, Compassionate and Benevolent Protector of the State and Shelterer of the People, Exalter of Blessings and Bestower of Vast Grace**,
and
**The Perfected Lord of the Nine Heavens’ Jade Portal, Proclaimer of Transformation and Upholder of the Teachings, Supreme Immortal of Radiant Numinosity, Vast Salvation, Lofty Clarity, Vast Stillness, Profound Serenity, Wondrous Response, Benevolent and Merciful Assistant to the State and Guardian of the People, Bestower of Abundant Blessings and Vast Grace**,
who assist the Dipper Perfected at the Northern Culmen
and inwardly participate in the Mysteries of the Eastern Flower.
Through a hundred million kalpas, they cultivate without cease.
Fifty-five vows, each vow fulfilled in deliverance.
Refining gold into phoenix scripts, kneading jade to inscribe dragon chapters.
May all sentient beings together ascend the Supreme Dao.

The assembly of this Dao altar bows their heads in reverence, devoting their hearts to praise.
In unison, we chant the *Hymn of the Perfected Lords’ Original Vows*:

Ascending the imperial throne, advancing upon the celestial steps.
Radiance dependent on sun and moon, office encompassing the Three Terraces.
The ranked stars pay homage; the Han’s luminaries revolve in splendor.
The Dragon’s Horn in the east alone claims the Dipper’s head.
The Flowery Canopy and Chamber Steeds serve as strict and bright attendants.
The Feathered Forest Generals escort left and right.
The ocarina and reed-pipe play in alternation; the pitch-pipes harmonize in sound.
Returning in glory to the Celestial Palace, a journey of ten thousand leagues through the clouds.

**Response:**
The assembly of this Dao altar, each with utmost devotion, offers reverence according to the rites.

With devoted hearts, we prostrate and take refuge, honoring:
One whose virtue matches Heaven and Earth, whose merit parallels sun and moon,
whose numinous efficacy is wondrous, whose nature is upright and perceptive,
great in compassion, great in mercy, great in sageliness, great in vows,
who responds to conditions and answers prayers, who vows to deliver all beings—
**The Perfected Lord of the Nine Heavens’ Golden Portal, Illuminator of the Dao and Attainer of Virtue, Great Immortal Manifesting Numinous Pervasive Salvation, Pure and Subtle Cavernous Mystery, Void and Wondrous Response, Compassionate and Benevolent Protector of the State and Shelterer of the People, Exalter of Blessings and Bestower of Vast Grace.**

With devoted hearts, we prostrate and take refuge, honoring:
One whose might shakes thunder, whose grace descends like rain and dew,
whose numinous power is unobstructed, whose blessed virtue is boundless,
great in compassion, great in mercy, great in sageliness, great in vows,
who responds to the year’s cycles and answers prayers, who vows to deliver all beings—
**The Perfected Lord of the Nine Heavens’ Jade Portal, Proclaimer of Transformation and Upholder of the Teachings, Supreme Immortal of Radiant Numinosity, Vast Salvation, Lofty Clarity, Vast Stillness, Profound Serenity, Wondrous Response, Benevolent and Merciful Assistant to the State and Guardian of the People, Bestower of Abundant Blessings and Vast Grace.**

The Dao, majestic and ineffable,
the flourishing qi of the Nine Heavens belongs to the Perfected Lords.
From ancient times to the present, without end,
their hundred thousand transformations wondrously pervade the numinous.

**Response:**
Now we humbly praise their sagely virtue,
may their awe-inspiring radiance witness this sincerity.
May all sentient beings together take refuge in the Supreme Dao.

With devoted hearts, we prostrate and take refuge, honoring:
One whose virtue matches Heaven and Earth, whose merit parallels sun and moon...

**And: Now we humbly praise their sacred virtue...**
With devoted hearts, we prostrate and take refuge, honoring:
One whose virtue matches Heaven and Earth...
**The Perfected Lord of the Nine Heavens’ Golden Portal...**
With devoted hearts, we prostrate and take refuge, honoring:
One whose might shakes thunder...
**The Perfected Lord of the Nine Heavens’ Jade Portal...**

In the ninth month, when the Longevity Festival arrives,
Clouds part to reveal the Golden Portal, ascending to the azure heavens.
Now I bow like a tiger before the Hall of Long Life,
Together we offer blessings for a hundred myriad years of Yao’s reign.
**And: Now we humbly praise their sacred virtue...**
With devoted hearts, we prostrate and take refuge, honoring:
One whose virtue matches Heaven and Earth...
**The Perfected Lord of the Nine Heavens’ Golden Portal...**
With devoted hearts, we prostrate and take refuge, honoring:
One whose might shakes thunder...
**The Perfected Lord of the Nine Heavens’ Jade Portal...**

Joyfully encountering the grand celebration of the Middle Prime Festival,
Divine beings descend upon Mount Song, releasing the earth’s numen.
At the royal portal, golden censers waft fragrant smoke,
Colored clouds bear forth the Old Man Star.
**And: Now we humbly praise their sacred virtue...**
With devoted hearts, we prostrate and take refuge, honoring:
Within the Hall of Numinous Aid, in the Hall of Joyous Feasting,
Her nature endowed with modesty and gentleness, her beneficence equal to Earth’s depth,
She diligently upholds the virtue of the inner court, silently assisting in yin merits,
Her feathered canopy and rainbow robes inscribed with purple characters among the female immortals of Mount Goushi,
In golden chambers and jade halls, she received the *Yellow Court* before the Southern Marchmount’s Lady,
Her blessings extend to all beings, her sacrifices endure for a hundred generations,
Most sacred, most numinous, most yielding, most tranquil,
The Lady of Jing State, True and Responsive Divine Consort, Benevolent and Kindly Immortal Concubine.

Crowned with a golden diadem bearing the Seven Stars,
Seven dragons and five phoenixes jubilantly welcome her.
May she offer jade nectar and golden libations,
Pouring as rain and dew upon the human world.
With devoted hearts, we prostrate and take refuge, honoring:
Within the Hall of Numinous Aid, in the Hall of Joyous Feasting.

She personally upholds frugality, her governance marked by diligent care,
Thereby providing the good of the inner court’s virtue, assisting in Earth’s demeanor,
The search for a virtuous lady, free from deceit or private solicitation,
The crowing cock heralds the attainment of a worthy consort,
Thus exemplifying the way of mutual caution and mutual completion,
Her merits perfected in inner assistance, her virtue extending to all beings,
Most sacred, most numinous, most yielding, most tranquil,
The Lady of Wei State, True and Responsive Divine Consort, Kindly and Serene Immortal Concubine.

Attended by jade maidens as messengers,
The inner palace’s music and governance are perfectly complete.
All things rely on her for life, none fail to prosper,
Most yielding, most tranquil, she matches Earth’s origin.
With devoted hearts, we prostrate and take refuge, honoring:
Within the Hall of Numinous Aid, in the Hall of Harmonious Kinship.

Nothing is more solemn than a father, and what matches Heaven must be known,
No repayment suffices for such kindness, yet there exists a way of reverent rule,
Moreover, in serving the king and fulfilling his mandate, she answers and extols the glory of civil and martial achievements,
Establishing the state and founding the household, she alone bears the trust of Yi and Zhou,
Her merits secure the altars of soil and grain, her blessings extend to descendants,
Most sacred, most numinous, most venerable, most solemn,
The Divine Father, Prince of Qi, Loyal and Martial Illustrious True Lord.

The *Book of Songs* and *Book of Rites* were earnestly taught in the hall where carp were leapt,
Her inner assistance in the household was most strict and bright.
Before the hall, she learned the play of the patterned robe,
Offering longevity blessings for a thousand springs, presenting the rhinoceros-horn cup.
With devoted hearts, we prostrate and take refuge, honoring:
Within the Numinous Palace, in the Hall of Harmonious Kinship,
Most sagely, most kind, most wise, most serene and devoted,
Her position upright in the central palace, her merits perfected in inner assistance,
Her frugal virtue manifest, transforming those below, her illustrious deeds recorded in poetry and song,
Her yin rites cultivated, her teachings transforming, her fragrant name shining in the historical records,
Having cherished her parents’ loving kindness, she dared to express the household’s joyous rites,
Most sacred, most numinous, most compassionate, most loving,
The Divine Mother, Benevolent and Longevous, Kind and Good Immortal Consort.

Her mother’s toil must never be forgotten,
How vast is Earth’s virtue, boundless in harmony.
Forever adhering to her mother’s teachings, transmitting the household’s prosperity,
She chants the four chapters of “Thinking of Equality.”
With devoted hearts, we prostrate and take refuge, honoring:
Within the Hall of Aid, in the Hall of Harmonious Kinship,
Ocarina and flute play in alternation, their wings mutually completing,
Possessing both civil and martial talents, embodying the principles of brotherly and fraternal harmony,
Enfeoffed with land and titles, guarding the marches, granted the honor of increased fiefs,
Exalting virtue and repaying merit, simultaneously bestowed with royal titles,
Loving one another without resentment, ample and abundant,
Most sacred, most numinous, most fraternal, most loving,
The Divine Brothers, the Ennobled Princes in Array.

Before the Hall of Flourishing Blossoms, the village of accumulated goodness,
In former years, they were simultaneously granted royal titles,
A household of filial piety and fraternal love, their lofty integrity commended,
Their benevolent legacy endures for a thousand years in the Hall of Harmonious Kinship.
With devoted hearts, we prostrate and take refuge, honoring:
Within the Hall of Numinous Aid, in the Hall of Joyous Feasting,
Her curtains and skirts immaculately ordered, her silk screens arrayed in solemnity,
The household reveres the wife’s honored rites, as the love of Lady Zhong was recorded in literature,
She was known for the talents of a daughter of the Xie family, renowned for her virtue,
Combining the beauty of Lady Zhong, personally upholding the Four Teachings,
Her blessings bestowed upon the common people,
Most sacred, most numinous, most yielding, most tranquil,
The Divine Brothers’ Sacred Consorts in Array.

Reverently serving her mother’s countenance, delighting in fraternal harmony,
The hall filled with harmonious qi, smiling and joyful,
Distinctions of seniority preserved in the household’s prosperity,
Even slightly improper caps are not admitted to the censer.
With devoted hearts, we prostrate and take refuge, honoring:
Within the Hall of Numinous Aid, in the Hall of Harmonious Kinship,
Her descendants perpetuate abundance, their fragrance transmitted for a hundred generations,
Her children and grandchildren are worthy, displaying the refinement of orchids and irises,
The ancestral grand affairs rejoice in the preservation of hairpins and hairpieces,
Singing the poem of the creeping vine, chanting the virtue of the louse,
Most sacred, most numinous, most compliant, most reverent.

The divine sons and divine grandsons, the ranks of dukes and marquises.
The legacy of purity and integrity endures in their teachings,
Their renown resounds, their gates towering in grandeur.
Dukes and marquises bear the lineage of dukes and marquises,
For hidden merits inherently reside in their descendants.
With devoted hearts, we prostrate and take refuge, honoring:
Within the Hall of Numinous Aid, in the Hall of Harmonious Kinship,
Their teachings uphold the great ethical principles,
Harmonizing the three branches of kinship,
Receiving Heaven’s blessings,
Feasting on a thousand measures, even ten thousand measures,
Enfeoffed upon the earth,
First among those of the same surname, then among those of different surnames,
Having humbly received the profound love of General Liu Hong,
And knowing the prudent virtue of the honorable Fu Zheng,
Their names weigh heavily in their time,
Their rewards extend through the ages,
Most sacred, most numinous, most kindred, most benevolent—the divine uncles and divine sons-in-law, the ranks of dukes and marquises.

The maternal uncle of Weiyang, kin to the mother,
Once knew the brilliance of pearls and jade.
Further compiling the works of Han Yu in order,
Li Han’s literary fame spread far and wide.
With devoted hearts, we prostrate and take refuge, honoring:
Within the Hall of Numinous Aid, in the Hall of Swallowing Joy,
The inner chambers are solemn and orderly,
The laws and disciplines strictly observed,
Whether abundant or scarce,
Their aspirations lie in women’s work,
Gathering duckweed and pondweed,
Teaching that refined virtue comes first,
Rites dictate devotion to parents-in-law,
Filial piety never forgets one’s own parents,
Most sacred, most numinous, most reverent, most compliant—the divine daughters and divine daughters-in-law, the ranks of immortal consorts.

The seven chapters of the *Nü Jie* follow in harmony,
Whether to uncles or parents-in-law, they are as to parents.
Delighted to wear the gifts of orchids and mallows,
They diligently uphold the virtue of wives, solemn and harmonious.
With devoted hearts, we prostrate and take refuge, honoring:
Within the Hall of Numinous Aid, in the Hall of Swallowing Joy,
Beneath cloud-canopied pavilions, they wander freely,
In the Moon Palace, they enjoy wealth and nobility,
Their robes flow gracefully,
Adorning themselves with trailing garments and osmanthus skirts,
Their forms towering,
Adorned with bright pearls and golden kingfisher plumes,
How beautiful, how radiant,
Gentle and resplendent.
May they channel the numinous power of Mount Wu,
Forever serving as the auspicious omens of this blessed land,
Most sacred, most numinous, free and unbound—the assembled ranks of sacred consorts within the hall.

Pearl-slippered and golden-haired, they fill the palace courtyards,
Their demeanor rich, their intentions profound, refined and true.
Gathering duckweed from the ponds, as befits the affairs of dukes and marquises,
Unlike the imperial consort’s chambers, famed as those of the Qin.
With devoted hearts, we prostrate and take refuge, honoring:
Within the Hall of Numinous Aid, in the Hall of Swallowing Joy,
The sun as their soul, the moon as their spirit,
The Great Unity oversees the register of births,
The Heavenly Unity governs the office of life-bestowing,
The constellations store essence,
Inspiring dreams through the Evening Star,
Mountains and rivers nurture brilliance,
Rejoicing in the descent of the sacred peaks,
Embracing the qilin from Heaven above,
Becoming the phoenixes of the human realm,
Most sacred, most numinous, responsive to every invocation.

The Divine Overseers of the Great Unity’s Birth Register,
The Divine Overseers of the Heavenly Unity’s Life-Bestowing Office,
The assembled ranks of consorts.
What joy in auspicious dreams—playing with jade scepters,
The auspicious qi of Mount Ao shines forth.
Children beget grandchildren, grandchildren beget children,
A hundred generations of the main branch flourish and prosper.
With devoted hearts, we prostrate and take refuge, honoring:
In the courtyard of the Dragon’s Head Temple, in the sacred realm of Mount Ao,
Their duties encompass the hundred officials,
Their ranks among the nine ministers,
The Controller of Emoluments wields the scales of Wenchang,
The Master of Blessings governs the life-bestowing authority,
Their teachings follow the *Hong Fan*:
"Long life, wealth, health, and peace."
Their praises resound in the ancestral temple,
Bringing prosperity, flourishing, and longevity,
Each person rejoices,
Everywhere receives grace,
Most sacred, most numinous, echoing like response to sound—the divine overseers of left and right blessings and emoluments.

The twin stars of Blessing and Emolument appear at the pivot of the Dipper,
Their duties lie in advancing the worthy through the imperial examinations.
Esteemed families, accumulating goodness, are called gentlemen,
Their children and grandchildren overflow with blessings.
With devoted hearts, we prostrate and take refuge, honoring:
In the courtyard of the Dragon’s Head Temple, in the sacred realm of Mount Ao,
Lightning flashes brilliantly,
Clouds rise high,
Heaven speaks not, yet its voice thunders in wrath,
The earth’s bounty relies on rain and dew to nurture life,
Divine mechanisms operate in the unfathomable,
Wondrous transformations turn in the formless,
Grace extends to the nine regions,
Blessings cover all living beings,
Most sacred, most numinous, ever-changing, ever-transforming—
Lord Thunder and Mother Lightning,
Earl Wind and Master Rain,
The luminous spirits of this palace,
The trustworthy Dragon Kings of Aid,
And the local earth deities of the five directions,
The rain-bringing dragon spirits, and all others.

Dragons ride the clouds, inherently numinous,
Their voices shake the thunder for ten thousand miles.
The world’s multitudes yearn for timely rain,
Suddenly their horns rise, towering and majestic.
With devoted hearts, we prostrate and take refuge, honoring:
In the sacred realm of Mount Ao, in the courtyard of the Dragon’s Head Temple,
Most sacred, most divine,
To the left, to the right,
Some present the arts of jesters,
Others excel in the skills of charioteers,
The stewards of the kitchen employ the eight delicacies,
The masters of music harmonize the six pitches,
The sixteen guards of the army are all generals in the making,
The three hundred cavalrymen each bear the marks of marquises,
Their might and numinosity resplendent,
Their images fierce and awe-inspiring,
Most sacred, most numinous, stern and protective,
The assembled ranks of the hall, the assembled ranks of the hall,
Mighty and numinous, mighty and numinous.

For their labors in stabilizing the state and benefiting the people,
Their incense and karmic ties are enshrined in the temple.
The fame of generals and ministers endures through the ages,
Their images praised for a thousand years like the qilin.
We kneel in reverence,
Sincerely repenting.
With devoted hearts, we surrender our bodies and take refuge,
Prostrating before the Nine Heavens’ Numinous Aid Perfected Lord,
And the assembled might and numinous immortals of the hall.

We humbly beseech the sacred compassion to bestow great blessings,
Showering vast grace,
As today, with solemn devotion,
We prostrate in repentance.
We have heard that misfortune and fortune have no fixed gate,
Only summoned by one’s own actions.
Good and ill omens appear,
Like shadows following form.
Goodness is the tally of evil,
Evil is the proof of goodness.
For those who do good,
The five phases support them,
The Controller of Fate befriends them.
For those who do evil,
Malevolent qi overwhelms them,
Evil stars shine upon them.
Though the Heavenly Net is inescapable,
It lies in the awakening of the human heart.
Today, we reflect upon all sentient beings,
Turning their hearts toward the Dao,
Sincerely invoking the divine,
Bowing in reverence to the truly wise.
First confessing our faults,
From past kalpas to this present life,
We have been ashamed of our transgressions, committing wrongs,
Turning from compliance to rebellion,
Altering our nature, clinging to obstinacy,
Employing deceit to exploit fissures,
Acting with dark cunning and perversity to carry out treachery,
Exercising cruelty and savagery to inflict harm.

Deluded by dreams and illusions, they wander lost in the pursuit of profit and fame.
Their wills are ensnared in the fields of killing, theft, deceit, and lust,
Sunk deep in the realms of greed, hatred, and delusion.
In great matters, they deceive Heaven and Earth;
In hidden ways, they betray the gods and spirits.
They curse the scorching heat and resent the cold,
Rebuke the wind and revile the rain.
At times, they relieve themselves beneath the stars,
Or expose themselves naked before the sun and moon.
They point at rainbows, swear oaths by mountains and seas,
Desecrate temples and shrines, defile sacred precincts.
Unmindful of the transgressions of body, heart, speech, and intent,
They disregard the proper roles of scholar, farmer, artisan, and merchant.
They neither honor the Three Treasures nor cultivate the Five Constants.
In serving others, they are disloyal;
In friendship, they are untrustworthy.
Toward parents, they are unfilial;
Toward lords, they are ungrateful.
The wealthy lack benevolence;
Those who hoard wealth lack righteousness.
They claim sacrifices are futile,
That violence causes no harm,
That reverence is not worth practicing,
That words are not to be feared.
They rebel against superiors and stir up chaos,
Flaunt their strength and resent poverty.
They slander and entrap the loyal and good,
Bully the orphaned and weak.
They suppress the public for private gain,
Exalt themselves while belittling others,
Incite lawsuits and sow enmity.
They mock and humiliate the innocent,
Act in ignorance of goodness,
And lack sincerity in themselves.
Minor transgressions may sever the bond between father and son,
Or dissolve the affection between brothers.
When the customs of the state decay, the lament of *Gufeng* arises;
When kin turn against one another, the song of *Jiaogong* is sung.
Now, recognizing the full measure of their sins,
They bow in reverence before the compassionate and repent in sorrow.
Who among men is without fault?
Yet if one errs and then reforms,
One should ever tremble with fear.
The gods do not accept offerings unconditionally,
But only those made with utmost sincerity.
With humble and earnest devotion,
They prostrate themselves, praying that the Most Benevolent may grant protection,
That the Great Dao may show mercy,
Forgiving past transgressions
And bestowing future blessings.
May all regions rejoice,
And all lands receive grace.
May this day bring great peace,
With no disasters arising, no calamities befalling,
And all things of fortune arriving in full.
May the old grow strong,
The young grow vigorous,
And the awe-inspiring virtue of the divine spirits be long revered,
So that their works may aid the people.
With utmost sincerity, we bow twice in worship and give thanks
To the Two True Lords of Lingji.
*Rise.*
Disciples, with one heart, bow in worship and give thanks
To the True Lord of Vast Grace of the Nine Heavens’ Golden Portal.
Disciples, with one heart, bow in worship and give thanks
To the True Lord of Vast Grace of the Nine Heavens’ Jade Portal.
Disciples, with one heart, bow in worship and give thanks
To the Sacred Father, True Lord of Loyalty and Martial Brilliance.
Having laid bare our earnest wishes, we humbly pray that the Sacred Compassion may deign to look upon us.

We offer ten prayers:
First, may the present Emperor’s longevity be as boundless as Heaven, harmonizing thus:
*May his years match Heaven’s, ten thousand springs in endless bliss.*
Second, may the ministers and officials enjoy rank and emolument, harmonizing thus:
*May wind and cloud bring a thousand years of joyous prosperity.*
Third, may the scholars attain wealth and nobility, harmonizing thus:
*May their names ascend to Heaven’s court as dukes and ministers.*
Fourth, may the farmers diligently till the soil, harmonizing thus:
*From this year onward, may each harvest bring triple abundance.*
Fifth, may the artisans perfect their crafts, harmonizing thus:
*May they await the imperial summons at the palace gates, hearing the jade tones of decree.*
Sixth, may the path to wealth be broad and true, harmonizing thus:
*May a thousand households be enfeoffed as lords, their ranks unmatched.*
Seventh, may wind and rain be timely and harmonious, harmonizing thus:
*May all under Heaven rejoice in peace and prosperity.*
Eighth, may the incense fires ever flourish, harmonizing thus:
*May the temple’s majesty and divine power endure for a thousand years.*
Ninth, may the Nine Heavens bestow their mandate, harmonizing thus:
*May jade pendants chime as they approach the Purple Throne.*
Tenth, may all faithful and good beings in the ten directions, harmonizing thus:
*Return to the Three Treasures, each with utmost devotion.*

The rites of worship and hymns of praise are now complete.
All in the Daoist assembly, with reverence, once more address the spirits:
We have heard that with trembling caution, we dare not presume upon your patience,
Yet with awe and clarity, we behold your majestic presence before us.
With hearts inscribed by gratitude, we bow and raise our voices.
The virtues that shine forth are called manifest and luminous power;
Their merits may be extended to become universal and boundless salvation.
They serve as a bridge for the suffering,
A light for the lost in darkness.
Today, in this rite of gratitude and prayer for blessings,
We humbly stand before the True and Wise,
Proclaiming the wondrous teachings.
We offer the respect of triple ablutions and triple incense,
Yet cannot exhaust the reverence of even a single glance or bow.
The gods hear without partiality,
And our sincerity is plain before them.
May they cleanse the sins of past kalpas and this present life,
And let these acts become the causes of blessings in this life and the next.
With beginning and end complete,
Without evil or blemish,
What can be grasped, the foolish may yet attain;
What lies beyond, even the wise cannot fathom.
The gods transform, and the people are rightly guided.
When merit is fulfilled and deeds perfected,
One may ascend to the Jade Chamber and Cinnabar Terrace.
With qi preserved and spirit aligned,
One may open the brocade pouch of the Purple Yang.
May all faithful men and women attain long life,
And their ancestors of a hundred thousand generations all receive deliverance.
May even the departed in the hidden realms,
And all beings of every kind,
Return to the vast and boundless Great Vehicle.
For the supreme cause, we chant the invocation of the Heavenly Worthy.
The rites for the True Lords are now complete.

The Rite of the Seven Stars of the Celestial Balance is observed.
Today, we burn incense in offering to
The Great Immortal of the Nine Heavens’ Golden Portal, Illuminator of the Dao, Attainer of Virtue, Manifest Spirit of Universal Salvation, Pure and Subtle, Void and Wondrous, Compassionate and Benevolent, Protector of the State and Shelter of the People, True Lord of Vast Grace and Exalted Blessings;
The Supreme Immortal of the Nine Heavens’ Jade Portal, Propagator of Transformation, Upholder of the Teachings, Radiant Spirit of Boundless Salvation, Lofty and Serene, Profound and Wondrous, Kind and Benevolent, Assistant to the State and Benefactor of the People, True Lord of Vast Grace and Abundant Blessings;
The Divine Immortals within the Palace,
And all the Spirit Officials—
We make offerings to all alike.

We reverently recall that when the Dragon Han unfolded the cosmic chart,
The primordial qi of the Mysterious and Original divided.
When the great turtle bore the transformations of all things,
The positions of Heaven, Earth, and Man were established.
For mankind, the Great Dao is hard to encounter,
And to be born in the Middle Land is rare.
Moreover, we are endowed with yang and yin,
Our four limbs formed.
We must value our bodies, preserve our lives,
And keep the myriad qi ever present.
Yet we fear old age, sickness, and death,
And each rejoices in growing tall and fair.
Man has desires, but Heaven shows no partiality.
Why are some granted wealth, while others suffer poverty?
Why do some live long like Pengzu, while others die young like Yanling?
The numbers of fate’s allotment—why not seek them within ourselves?

At that time, the True Lords of Lingji were roaming and feasting in the Jade Pure Sacred Realm,
In the radiant reign of the August Emperor,
Under the luminous gaze of Heaven.

Having established the great karmic conditions, they expounded the teachings for the multitude.
The five celestial bodies I govern—now waxing, now waning—are never constant.
The two luminaries I traverse—one summer, one winter—follow their ordered sequence.
To follow them brings the joy of auspicious prosperity; to oppose them brings the sorrow of perilous calamity.
Only utmost sincerity can move the spirits, and thus the accumulation of good deeds must yield abundant blessings.
Bathed in the radiance of their illumination, how dare we forget the debt of gratitude we owe?
On this day, the devoted Daoist so-and-so reverently opens the sacred altar and presents humble offerings.
Following the Jade Calendar of Primordial Yang, he burns incense and recites scriptures.
In accordance with the present statutes of the Numinous Treasure, he observes the fast and upholds the precepts.
He elucidates the sacred canons and kindles the divine lamps.
Gazing upward at the warp and weft of the celestial texts, he envisions afar the forms of the armillary sphere.
The orchid incense burns bright—its blaze is seen, its embers unseen.
The iron vessel holds its oil—its increase is seen, its decrease unseen.
Above, it illumines the thirty-two heavens, its brilliance vast and boundless.
Below, it enables the multitudes of hundreds and thousands to behold, revere, and take refuge.

All good arises from within the light, all evil perishes within the light.
Bowing once and bowing again, the heart’s eye becomes clear and bright.
From the first offering of incense to the third, the chanting voices ring clear.
Gazing upward, we trust in your all-seeing gaze; looking down, we beseech your radiant grace.
May the Three Realms descend as one, and ten thousand people come in reverence.
Malevolent stars retreat and withdraw—throughout the four seasons, no harm nor calamity shall arise.
Auspicious luminaries approach the hall, bestowing the Five Blessings: fortune and longevity.
We bow our heads in homage, taking refuge in the ever-radiant Perfected Wondrous Dao and Virtue, the Heavenly Worthy of Constant Illumination.

The assembly, with sincere devotion, takes refuge and pledges faith to the Sacred Palace of Lingji:
The Heavenly Golden Portal’s Illuminated Dao and Attained Virtue Great Immortal, Manifestly Revealed and Universally Salvific, Pure Subtle Cavernous Mystery, Void and Wondrously Responsive, Compassionate and Benevolent Protector of the Nation and Shelter of the People, Exalted Blessing and Vast Grace Perfected Lord;
The Heavenly Jade Portal’s Proclaimed Transformation and Upholding Teaching Supreme Immortal, Illustrious and Vastly Salvific, Lofty and Illuminated, Vast and Serene, Void and Profound, Wondrously Responsive, Benevolent and Compassionate Assistant to the Nation and Protector of the People, Abundant Blessing and Vast Grace Perfected Lord;
The immortals within the palace, and all the numinous officials.

We reverently kindle the Seven Luminaries’ Divine Lamps of the Armillary Sphere, arranging above the image of the sun’s radiant yang.
We humbly recall: the Dao resides in the beginning of the Great Ultimate—unseen in its boundlessness, unmanifest in its subtlety.
The sun is the essence of all yang, fulfilling every aspiration and illuminating every hidden realm.
Its mystery is unfathomable, its presence divine.
Resplendent is its numinous power—men revere it as they did Zhao Dun.
Brilliant and ever-present above, the people gaze upon it as they did the Duke of Zhou.
Its virtue shines with radiance, vast indeed.
Its purity gleams like jade, bright and clear.
The crow-wheel is solemnly prepared, circling the palace of entangled ritual.
The chariot of Xi is majestically adorned, offering homage in the Hall of Cavernous Yang.
It emits a thousand-yard radiance, universally illuminating the three-thousandfold world.
Entering our gate, it dispels the doubt of the homeless.
Following our Dao, it eradicates the ailments of the forsaken path.

We reflect upon all sentient beings, lost in the dust and drowned in obscurity, vainly exhausting themselves in pursuit of shadows.
Like hail and dew, their splendor is fleeting—only the lament of passing moments remains.
From this day forth, may they turn inward and reflect, abiding in the Dao’s constant illumination.

We pray that those who trade in the marketplace may gain the wealth of merchants and shopkeepers.
Those who labor in the fields may find peace in plowing and well-digging.
The skilled artisan may measure shadows with the jade tablet.
The diligent craftsman may burn the midnight oil.
The scholar may compose verses in five-colored splendor.
The official may earn the title of the Eight Learned Scholars.
In the twilight of their years, may they vie with the pine and cypress in evergreen vitality.
May the glow of the firefly’s light increase, and may they share in the blessings bestowed upon all creatures.

With hearts as devoted as the sunflower’s turning, we beseech the bestowal of your radiant light.
The assembly now reverently follows the incantation of the Sun Sovereign as spoken by the Most High, bowing in homage and chanting with devotion.

With sincere hearts, we take refuge and pledge faith:
To the Heavenly Golden Portal’s Illuminated Dao and Attained Virtue Great Immortal, Manifestly Revealed and Universally Salvific, Pure Subtle Cavernous Mystery, Void and Wondrously Responsive, Compassionate and Benevolent Protector of the Nation and Shelter of the People, Exalted Blessing and Vast Grace Perfected Lord.
To the Heavenly Jade Portal’s Proclaimed Transformation and Upholding Teaching Supreme Immortal, Illustrious and Vastly Salvific, Lofty and Illuminated, Vast and Serene, Void and Profound, Wondrously Responsive, Benevolent and Compassionate Assistant to the Nation and Protector of the People, Abundant Blessing and Vast Grace Perfected Lord.

Forming the noon mudra, we inhale the noon qi.
From afar, we envision the Perfected Lord of the Cavernous Yang’s Resplendent Palace as if present.
Gazing eastward toward the Fusang Palace, we bow in homage to the Resplendent One.
O radiant light of the Cavernous Sun, vast and boundless—what thoughts arise?
Grant me the golden hue, awaiting the celestial vision of your majestic form.
The imperial blossoms and jade maidens descend to the hall at this very hour.

*Response:* May this lamp’s light be directed toward the Perfected Lord.
Scatter flowers.
The Heavenly Worthy of Great Illumination and Perfect Extremity.

The assembly, with sincere devotion, takes refuge and pledges faith to the Sacred Palace of Lingji:
The Heavenly Golden Portal’s Illuminated Dao and Attained Virtue Great Immortal, Manifestly Revealed and Universally Salvific, Pure Subtle Cavernous Mystery, Void and Wondrously Responsive, Compassionate and Benevolent Protector of the Nation and Shelter of the People, Exalted Blessing and Vast Grace Perfected Lord;
The Heavenly Jade Portal’s Proclaimed Transformation and Upholding Teaching Supreme Immortal, Illustrious and Vastly Salvific, Lofty and Illuminated, Vast and Serene, Void and Profound, Wondrously Responsive, Benevolent and Compassionate Assistant to the Nation and Protector of the People, Abundant Blessing and Vast Grace Perfected Lord;
The immortals within the palace, and all the numinous officials.

We reverently kindle the Seven Luminaries’ Divine Lamps of the Armillary Sphere, arranging above the image of the moon’s radiant yin.
We humbly recall: the primordial qi resides within the vastness of the Great Void—colorless and formless.
The moon’s essence descends with the splendor of blossoms, imbued with nature and sentiment.
Passing through the Winnowing Basket, it stirs the wind; departing from the Net, it brings forth rain.
Such is the work of Heaven.
Manifesting its numinous power through illumination.

With eighty-three thousand gates to the Toad Palace, its pure radiance may be drawn near. Gazing upon the Crane Terrace of fifteen hundred years, its sacred presence lingers still. When Liu Yuanshi broke the barbarian siege, his aspiration to ascend the tower was indeed fulfilled. When Cao Mengde forged his hegemony, what hindered him from strumming the zither and singing? Some, refining their essence, received the Han’s tally; others, yielding their luminance, answered Wu’s auspice. Their names resound with clarity, their deeds shine with distinction.

We humbly pray that all beings—those who steal light in fleeting shadows, or nurture obscurity within dust-laden concealment; those who conceal flaws while magnifying strengths, or who, masking faults with embellishment, incur the sin of dim confusion—may now offer forthright repentance and, by fortune, behold this luminous grace.

May the swans gather in the marsh without fear of ravenous flight, and within the realm where the cock crows, may the ox’s labored breath never be heard. Those who pound the hare’s elixir may attain long life; those who harvest the oyster’s pearl may gain wealth. Those who enter office may soon be chosen by the Moon Goddess; those betrothed may indeed await the Old Man’s word. When the Jade Light appears, may fine sons be conceived; when the jade adze is wielded, may craftsmanship reach perfection. Bowing in reverence to the Weaver Maid while marking the sundial, we shame ourselves before Venus’s raised cup.

The assembly of ritualists, in accordance with the *Divine Incantation of the Great Yin Sovereign Lord* as spoken by the Most High, prostrate in devotion and chant with sincere reverence:

*With wholehearted devotion, we take refuge and pay homage to the Lofty and Illuminated, Vast and Serene, Void and Profound, Wondrously Responsive, Benevolent and Compassionate Assistant to the Nation and Protector of the People, Abundant Blessing and Vast Grace Perfected Lord of the Golden Towers of the Nine Heavens.*

*With wholehearted devotion, we take refuge and pay homage to the Lofty and Illuminated, Vast and Serene, Void and Profound, Wondrously Responsive, Benevolent and Compassionate Assistant to the Nation and Protector of the People, Abundant Blessing and Vast Grace Perfected Lord of the Jade Towers of the Nine Heavens.*

Forming the mudra of the incantation, inhaling the unmanifest qi, we visualize the Perfected Lord of the Palace of Primal Yin’s Radiant Convergence as if present. Gazing upward to survey the eight directions, we see only the moon, pregnant with yin essence. Within it dwells the Primordial Sovereign, her lady attendants driving green carriages. Their splendor illumines the Two Poles, their blended radiance shines upon the Three Clarities. Earnestly seeking the supreme Dao, the Five Colors descend in welcome.

*Response:* May this lamp’s light be directed toward the Perfected Lord.
*Scatter flowers.*
*Perfect Mirror Illuminating Heaven Honored One.*

With wholehearted devotion, the assembly of ritualists takes refuge in the Numinous Aid Palace, the Golden Towers of the Nine Heavens, the Jade Towers of the Nine Heavens, the immortals within the palace, and all the numinous officials. We reverently kindle the Seven Luminaries’ Divine Lamps of the Armillary Sphere, arranging above the image of the Wood Virtue’s Year Star of the East.

We humbly recall: the heart of the Dao is one, profound and silent, beyond naming. The spirit of Wood is benevolence, its wondrous work the ceaseless generation of life. In time, it is spring, and the spring wind nurtures all; in virtue, it is the origin, and the primordial qi quickens the embryo. All equally receive its fostering power, yet still rely upon its pruning force. As the high mountain commands reverence, so too does this truth hold everywhere. Xie An, obtaining it, revealed the numinous power of Mount Gong; the Duke of Zhou, obtaining it, dispelled the slander of golden mounds. When Shuo was employed to harmonize the plum, dreams came from the wilds; when the mulberry was gathered and the corpse appeared, the spirit descended at Xin. Their achievements stood unmatched in their time, their names fragrant through ten thousand generations.

We humbly reflect upon all beings—those who, like the tree-stump watcher, cling to their lot, or who, like the parasitic vine, overreach their station. Though their timber be coarse and unadorned, like the oak or the uncarved block, yet if their nature is straight as the catalpa or the willow, their cups and trays may still serve. When guided by the marking-line, they are made straight; without the carpenter’s square, they cannot be formed.

We pray that those who hold office may carve their patterns with simplicity and elegance; that those who hear lawsuits may govern with the grace of the sweet pear. Observing the way of the catalpa and the catalpa-son, may fathers be kind and sons filial; singing the poem of the flowering calyx, may elder brothers be friendly and younger brothers respectful. May those who wish for sons become sagely younger brothers, sprouting the five-branched osmanthus; may those who form friendships become ageless companions, standing tall as the thousand-year pine. May the peach blossom with its radiance bring harmony to house and home; may the autumn fruit be offered in reverence to ancestors and forebears. Though we present the humble gift of dates, it is not to imitate the grand rite of burning offerings.

Let the assembly of ritual practitioners reverently follow the divine incantation of the Star Lord of Wood Virtue as spoken by the Most High, bowing their heads in homage and reciting with devout sincerity:

With wholehearted devotion, we take refuge and pay homage
To the Golden Towers of the Nine Heavens.
With wholehearted devotion, we take refuge and pay homage
To the Jade Towers of the Nine Heavens.

The incantation gathers the script of yín and hài, drawing the qi of yín and hài.
Envision the Perfected Lords of the Azure Flower Azure Heaven as though present.
The Year Star rides the virtue of Wood, revolving to illuminate the eastern quarter.
Its celestial form is moist and radiant, five hues blending in luminous splendor.
Seeking blossoms, they sing in vast waves; casting water, they chant in the chambers of mushrooms.
Through seasons of frequent prayers and supplications, blessings naturally grow everlasting.

Response: May this lamp’s light be turned toward the Perfected Lords.
Scatter flowers.
The Heavenly Worthy of Wondrous Wisdom and Perfect Illumination.

With wholehearted devotion, the assembly of ritual practitioners prostrate themselves before the efficacious powers of the Lingji Palace—
The Golden Towers of the Nine Heavens,
The Jade Towers of the Nine Heavens,
The immortals within the palace, and all divine officials.

Reverently kindling the Seven Luminaries Lamp of the Jade Balance, we array the image of the Fire Virtue Sparkling Deluder Star in the southern quarter.
We humbly recall that Fire holds the virtue of the southern quarter, where the Flame Emperor wields authority.
The deity governs as Lord of the Eastern Sea, and the Perfected Lord is granted his title.
His spirit is forged from jade essence, his form refined from golden elixir.
He studies the scriptures beyond the mundane, his goodness like a reflection in light.
Responding to circumstances, he transforms; vowing to deliver all beings,
He lifts those mired in suffering and places them upon his sleeping mat.
Moved by the scorched and parched multitudes, he turns their cries into songs of joy.
In laboring to stabilize the realm, the sunbird manifests auspicious signs.
In warding off calamities and repelling disasters, the Fire God reverses the winds.
His voice heralds radiant splendor, his majestic power blazes mightily.

We reflect upon all sentient beings: their desires remain unquenched, their study of the Dao unclear.
In their pursuit of power, they cannot avoid flattery to curry favor.
In their schemes, how dare they not resort to treachery and spread poison?
Trying to stop boiling by stirring the pot—is this not folly?
Gathering embers after the fire—is it not too late?
Fortunately, the warning to "bend the chimney and move the firewood" still stands;
Yet like snow touched to a red-hot furnace, the moment of awakening arrives.
Anxiety is like smoke—who can grasp heat?
Once a prairie fire spreads, can it be extinguished?
How can one allow jade to burn with it?

We humbly pray: may our weapons be stilled, the alarms of wolf-smoke forever silenced.
May the people’s suffering be relieved—what need is there for the labor of moxibustion?
May those who cook and drink find nourishment for life;
May those who gather firewood and tend stoves each secure their livelihood.

Heaven observes the singular virtue, thus it is said: "Sincerity leads to enlightenment, and enlightenment to sincerity."
By doing good, a hundred blessings descend, enabling you to flourish and thrive, thriving ever more.
A single stick of heart-incense may reach the azure heavens;
Three beams of divine light illuminate the sacred altar.
The assembly of ritualists, reverently invoking the Fire Virtue Star Lord’s incantation as spoken by the Most High, bow in homage and devotion, chanting in praise.

With devoted hearts, we pay homage and sincerely worship:
The Nine Heavens’ Golden Portal.
With devoted hearts, we pay homage and sincerely worship:
The Nine Heavens’ Jade Portal.

The incantation is formed with the *mao-xu* mudra, drawing the *qi* of *mao* and *xu*.
Envision the Palace of Vermilion Fire Refinement—may the True Lord be present as if in person.
Dragon and phoenix sprout sharp edges, their majestic radiance emanating in all ten directions.
Cinnabar hardness gleams through the five watches of night; vermilion flames blaze along the three borders.
Crystal clarity aligns with the upright *qi*; swords and halberds grasp the authority of arms.
Rushing and seizing, they respond by vanquishing the near; comets and broom stars dare not advance.

*Response:* May this lamp’s light be turned toward the True Lord.
Scatter flowers.
The wisdom torch blazes resplendent, Heavenly Worthy.

The assembly of ritualists, with devoted hearts, pay homage to the Divine Aid Palace:
The Nine Heavens’ Golden Portal,
The Nine Heavens’ Jade Portal,
The immortals within the palace,
And all the spirit officials.

Reverently kindling the Seven Luminaries Lamp of the Jade Balance, we present the image of the Earth Virtue Star of the Central Palace.
We have heard that in ancient rites, the earth was venerated at the altar, harmonizing with the earth’s proper order.
The virtue of the divine aligns with the Dao of Heaven.
Auspicious stone inscriptions were offered, and yin and yang prospered under the Tang;
Lucky clods appeared in the wild, and the gods lent their support to the Jin.
When Qin conquered Shu, the omens of Baogu Valley were no mere oddity;
When Liu swallowed Huan, the Xianbei’s dream was no coincidence.
The filial son of the Zong clan buried his father and revealed hidden merit;
The Iron-Wheel King’s acts of giving fulfilled karmic causes.
The great ship of Hong Gui may be relied upon—
The virtuous governance of Xu Jiang endures through the ages.
The sword of Lei Huan may shine ever brighter—
The sacred proximity of Huayin remains as if a thousand years have not passed.
Mixing sand with wine, it once served as a remedy for illness given to Prefect Gao;
Forming dust into pills, it once became a life-saving elixir from the immortals’ presence.
By virtue of Huang’s goodness, his numinous power is manifest.

We reflect upon all sentient beings: ants clinging to fleeting lives, wall-insects clinging to their dullness.
Evil abounds while good is scarce—how can there be no shortfall by even a single basket?
The Buddhas of the past have shown that even they could not avoid being reborn a hundred times.
To suppress demons in filth and dust—what use is there?
Yet if they wallow in the mire, can they truly be abandoned?

From this day forth, following the correct Dao in conduct, how dare we not build walls and rise in reverence?
We humbly pray:
May Mount Hua store its essence, so that scholars may be born with keen intelligence;
May gold be valued equally, so that merchants may prosper in trade.
May artisans refine their skills and reap the rewards of their labor;
May the pulse of fertile soil quicken, so that farmers may toil in the fields.
Striking the stone chimes and sounding the qing, we roughly perform the rites of drum and mallet;
Pouring water and offering flowers, we are ashamed to lack the tribute of finest jade.

The assembly of ritualists, reverently following the Earth Virtue Star Lord’s divine incantation as spoken by the Most High, bow in homage and devotion, chanting in earnest praise.

With devoted hearts, we pay homage and sincerely worship:
The Nine Heavens’ Golden Portal.
With devoted hearts, we pay homage and sincerely worship:
The Nine Heavens’ Jade Portal.

The incantation is formed with the *zi-chou* mudra, drawing the *qi* of *zi* and *chou*.
Envision the Palace of the Yellow Center’s Primordial *Qi*—may the True Lord be present as if in person.
The lofty heavens align with *wu* and *ji*; hidden lands rise through layered skies.
The Five Phases honor the obscured luminaries; the Nine Heavens reveal shining light.
Gan and Shi calculated the movements of Liu and Fu; Tao and Wu divined the depths of emptiness.
The immortals bestow rain and dew; prostrating on the earth, we bow to the empty void.

*Response:* May this lamp’s light be turned toward the True Lord.
Scatter flowers.
The divine light blazes resplendent, Heavenly Worthy.

The assembly of ritualists, with devoted hearts, pay homage to the Divine Aid Palace:
The Nine Heavens’ Golden Portal,
The Nine Heavens’ Jade Portal,
The immortals within the palace,
And all the spirit officials.

Reverently kindling the Seven Luminaries Lamp of the Jade Balance, we present the image of the Metal Virtue Star of the Western Palace, Venus.
We have heard that metal nurtures the essence of Venus, and the West bears its sign.
The divine ranks among the Upper Clarity; the Northern Dipper transforms its form.
Its literary brilliance has long shone on Tiantai; its origins trace back to the Lishui.
Poetry and odes possess a resounding beauty;
Its name inscribed on bells and tripods, it bears a nature of unyielding integrity.
Li Shaojun thereby refined the elixir; Shang’s Fu Yue used it to sharpen his resolve.
As a treasure, it is truly precious;
As an instrument, how could it be taken lightly?
The higher one gazes, the loftier it seems; the deeper one probes, the firmer it becomes.
It is sharply defined, yet harmoniously ordered.

We reflect upon all sentient beings: ashamed of the "four knowings," we admire Yang Zhen’s virtue in vain;
Unable to achieve even "three acquisitions," we vainly envy the wealth of Tao Zhu.
From this day forward, in forging and reforming, we truly rely on the power of smelting and shaping.
We humbly pray:
May scriptures and fruits remain unburned, and the teachings of the full basket bring joy;
May culture not yet be lost, and the sound of jade striking the ground still be heard.
If words can be acted upon and names spoken, the promises of the Chu people will be as steadfast as Ji Bu’s.
If sages emulate Heaven and worthies emulate sages, the disciples of Confucius will not be limited to Yan Hui alone.
Ashamed that we lack the grand treasures to present, we offer only the modest tribute of ritual vessels.

The assembled ritualists, in strict accordance with the divine incantation of the Golden Virtue Star Lord as expounded by the Most High, prostrate in reverent devotion and chant with sincere praise.

With wholehearted devotion, we take refuge and pay homage
To the Nine Heavens’ Golden Palaces.
With wholehearted devotion, we take refuge and pay homage
To the Nine Heavens’ Jade Palaces.

The incantation is formed with the *chen-you* mudra, drawing the *qi* of *chen* and *you*.
We visualize the True Lord of the Golden Heaven’s Luminous Palace as though present.

Venerable Venus ascends the limpid Han,
Frost-laden brilliance gleams with pristine radiance.
Lofty it floats in auspicious splendor,
Resplendent it shines as the resurgent Star of Longevity.
Its blade, towering, repels invaders;
Its hue, lustrous, ever subdues armies.
Exhaustively it accords with fate’s reckoning,
Uniting with the Dao to attain immortality.

*Response:* May this lamplight be directed toward the True Lord.
Scatter flowers.
The Radiant Nurturer of the Luminous Heavenly Venerable.

The assembled ritualists, with wholehearted devotion, prostrate and entrust their lives to the numinous efficacy of the Lingji Palace—
The Nine Heavens’ Golden Palaces,
The Nine Heavens’ Jade Palaces,
The immortals within the palaces,
And all the divine officials.

We reverently kindle the Seven Luminaries Lamp of the Celestial Balance,
Arranging above the constellation of the Northern Water Virtue’s *Chen* Star.
We have heard that the spirit of water is called Dark Depth,
Its source profound, its flow far-reaching.
Like water beneath the earth, where does it not reach?
Where does it not flow unimpeded?
Vast and boundless—how can I name its power?
Abyssal and fathomless—truly beyond measure.

Speak of its benevolence, and fish and turtles find their place.
Speak of its majesty, and dragons and spirits submit.
Whirling sands and bending waves once revealed the dream of the Three Isles.
Rising clouds and summoning rain are revered in the shrines of the Four Rivers.
Crossing the frozen Fen and Tuo, how divine were the words of kings and hegemons!
Leveling Huai and Cai with snow, was Li Su’s merit not heaven-sent?
All equally receive its moistening, downward-flowing kindness—
Dare we now make our plea to the Eastern Dawn?

We reflect upon all sentient beings:
At the Thieves’ Spring, they quench thirst—how gluttonous and unworthy!
The muddy Wei flows ever on, making foulness reek of itself.
We must earnestly cleanse and purify,
Lest we sink into dissipation.

We humbly pray:
May the courts enjoy peace, and the pearls return to Hepu.
May talents flourish and prosper, and boats cross mighty rivers.
When mulberries in the cleared groves ripen, silkworms will ascend early.
When swords in barren lands are sold, oxen may be raised.
The wellsprings of wealth and profit will accumulate—
Abundant, what more could be added? It is called enrichment.
The streams of descendants will flow long—
After great virtue, there must be those who rise.
May grace overflow like waves,
And blessings run as deep as the ocean.

We offer but the humble rites of transient streams,
Deeply ashamed of the meagerness of hoofprints in a puddle.

The assembled ritualists, in strict accordance with the divine incantation of the Water Virtue Star Lord as expounded by the Most High, prostrate in reverent devotion and chant with sincere praise.

With wholehearted devotion, we take refuge and pay homage
To the Nine Heavens’ Golden Palaces.
With wholehearted devotion, we take refuge and pay homage
To the Nine Heavens’ Jade Palaces.

The incantation is formed with the *si-shen* mudra, drawing the *qi* of *si* and *shen*.
We visualize the True Lord of the Dark Numinous Palace of Great Virtue as though present.

Wondrous! The tally of the Five *Qi*,
Dimly we perceive the True Gate.
Towering, it stands in the *chou* position,
The *ren* and *gui* spirits of the cavernous depths.
Its radiance divides and congeals in purity,
Its gaze and offering attend our devout remembrance.
Immortal songs and dances accompany the Dao,
After a long while, descending from the Golden Heaven.

*Response:* May this lamplight be directed toward the True Lord.
Scatter flowers.
The Dragon Virtue Universally Illuminating Heavenly Venerable.

Reciting scriptures and incantations,
The merits of the lamp-lighting just performed are now complete.

We have heard that observing the celestial patterns reveals human affairs, enabling foresight.
Cultivating human affairs in accord with celestial patterns brings unerring auspiciousness.
We must rely on the divine lamp for illumination,
And specially invoke the ritual canons for proclamation.
We redirect these merits to the True Lords,
Humbly beseeching their numinous favor.

From this day forward, may their power be grandly manifested.
We humbly pray:
May stars gather in *Kui*, and we again witness the governance of literary brilliance.
May light be contained in *Bi*, and the pristine customs of antiquity return.
Above, may they embody Heaven’s intent;
Below, may they fulfill the people’s hopes.

Furthermore, after the lighting of the lamps,
May the Five Planets follow their proper courses, and the Two Luminaries increase in splendor.
May cold and heat not stray from their seasons,
And all people be raised to benevolence and longevity.
May rain and sunshine arrive in due time,
And the hundred grains enjoy abundant harvests.
May all creatures with consciousness
Be nurtured by transformation.

We rely upon the vast assembly,
To forge the finest karmic affinity.

*Recitation:*

The Three Pure Ones and the Two Realms Heavenly Worthies,
The Nine Heavens’ Bestowers of Blessings Heavenly Worthies,
The Ten Directions’ Numinous Treasure Heavenly Worthies—
Whose merits are beyond all thought.

The *Star-Lamp Rite of the Seven Celestial Regulators* now complete,
The *Secret Canon of the Immortal Consorts* enters the altar.
*Stepping the Void:*
At the dawn of primordial chaos,
Yin and yang transformed and gave birth.
The Nine Heavens perfected the Dao’s transformation,
And the myriad lands preserved peace.

The jeweled throne descends upon the golden hall,
Crimson coronets radiate in the jade pavilion.
The ten thousand perfected gather at the imperial abode,
Soaring on rainbow hues with roots of luminous blossoms.

*Offering of Incense:*
Auspicious smoke coils into talismanic script,
Fortunate qi congeals in the void.
Gazing toward the azure vault, we pledge sincerity;
Beholding the Purple Clarity, we bow in reverence.
With reverence, we offer the incense of the Dao,
The incense of virtue,
The incense of non-action,
The pure incense of non-action,
The naturally pure incense,
The wondrous cavernous true incense,
The numinous treasure’s gracious incense,
The incense transcending the Three Realms—
Filling the jasper towers and jade halls,
Pervading all celestial immortal realms.
In utmost devotion, we present these offerings to:
The Heavenly Mother of the Nine Heavens, the Supreme Empress of the Primordial Lord;
The Empress of Earth, the August Thearch of the Sustaining Soil, who responds to the vast assembly;
The Holy Mother of the Eight Poles, Governess of the Law and Benevolent Abode;
The Eastern Pole’s Life-Preserving Holy Mother, the Azure-Clad Empress;
The Southern Pole’s Nurturing Holy Mother, the Empress of Fiery Radiance;
The Holy Mother of the Eight Poles, Overseer of Rectitude, the Golden Radiance Empress;
The Great Heavenly Web’s Grand Assembler, the Mystic Truth Empress;
The Nine Heavens’ Inspector and Examiner, the Demon-Subduing Empress;
The Governing Mistress of the Jambudvīpa World, the Illustrious Jade Pillar, the Sixfold Penetration Empress;
The Nine Heavens’ Opener of Transformation and Nurturer of Life, the Benevolent Consort;
The Illustrious Consort Wang;
The Azure Virtue Consort;
The Illustrious Consort Wan;
The Nine Heavens’ Opener of Transformation, the Loyal Virtue Consort;
The Illustrious Consort Yan;
The Lady of Jing State, who aids with benevolent compliance and chaste responsiveness;
The Lady of Wei State, who assists with kind wisdom and reverent tranquility;
The Holy Mother of the Harmonious Hall, the Benevolent and Longevous, the Refined and Kind Immortal Consort;
The Illustrious Consort Xiao of the Tang King’s Court;
The Benevolent Immortal Consort of the Hong King’s Court;
The Compliant and Gracious Immortal Consort of the E King’s Court;
The Auspicious Immortal Consort of the Guangling King’s Court;
The Pure and Gracious Immortal Consort;
The Illustrious and Gracious Immortal Consort;
The Kind and Gracious Lady;
The Gentle and Yielding Lady;
The Benevolent and Compliant Lady;
The Illustrious and Gracious Lady;
The Compliant and Reverent Lady;
The Illustrious and Wise Lady;
The Reverent and Gracious Lady;
The Serene and Gracious Lady;
The Illustrious and Harmonious Lady;
The Compassionate and Filial Lady;
The Holy Matrons and all the Ladies;
The Attendant Ladies of the Inner Court: the Compliant and Accomplished Lady,
the Illustrious Splendor Lady,
the Comely Lady,
the Cultivated Countenance Lady,
the Cultivated Demeanor Lady,
the Illustrious Demeanor Lady;
The Inner Canon’s Matrons of Merit;
The Silk and Hemp Ladies;
The Reed Storehouse Ladies;
The Curtain Assemblers;
The Treasury Ladies;
The Palace Scribes and all the Ladies;
The Female Invokers and Female Attendants, all the Noblewomen;
The Inner Attendants and Inner Canon’s Holy Kin Ladies;
The Heavenly Concubine who Registers Births;
The Great Unity’s Overseer of Auspicious Births;
The Ladies of the Three Offices: the Controller of Emoluments,
the Controller of Lifespans,
the Supreme Minister;
The Chamber-Guarding and Womb-Protecting Lady;
The Life-Protecting and Womb-Safeguarding Lady;
The Ladies of the Left and Right, Nurturers of Kindness;
The Protecting and Transmitting Lady;
The Ladies of the Left and Right, Assemblers of the Court;
The Palace Seal-Holding Ladies;
The Embracing and Delivering Lady;
The Nursing and Nurturing Lady;
The Nurturing and Rearing Lady;
The Rebirth Transforming Grannies;
The Eastern and Western Ranks of the Joyous Hall, all the Ladies;
The Granny Officials: the Registrar of Blessings Wang,
the Registrar of Records,
the Registrar of Longevity;
The Governing Granny who Judges and Delivers;
The Womb-Guarding and Chamber-Protecting Grannies.

The Queen Mother’s Palace hosts seven thousand disciples,
The Waterside Enfeoffment of the Vast Blessings Chen Fifteen Ladies,
The Thirty-Six Palace Grannies.

Moreover, that which is beyond knowing is called the divine—
Responsive when moved,
The people to this day receive its bounty,
Yet none may forget.

To this day, we have attained such blessings—daring not to invoke the Mandate of the Supreme Emperor. With utmost reverence and awe, I bow my head again and again, humbly acknowledging the formless beyond, the essence of the Supreme Dao.

The Yellow Emperor unlocked its gates and drew forth its bolts;
The Most High Lord Lao transmitted its lamp and continued its seal.
Virtue yet not virtue—pure emptiness, wondrous and strange,
The silent void without origin,
Mystery upon mystery,
Vast and boundless,
The marvelous workings of generation upon generation.
It courses through the Six Voids without cease,
Governing the myriad things without omission.
How majestic its accomplishments—
No words suffice to praise its awe-inspiring power.

I reflect that my aspirations seek the Dao,
Yet my talents fall short of others.
In presenting this petition with words,
Even the steps of my heart’s ground,
I wish to borrow diligent reverence for my duty,
That I may not transgress the divine majesty within a foot’s reach.

Further considering we, the ritual leaders,
Have devoted ourselves to the sacred threads,
Invoking blessings through the temple of Lingji,
Our names recorded in illustrious enfeoffment.
Resounding is its fame,
Radiant its numinous power.
Harmonious within the palace,
Solemn within the temple.
Though mulberry and catalpa command reverence,
Only the humble offerings of duckweed may be presented.
On this morning of Zhongyuan, when blessings are gathered,
It is also the dawn of the Prime Minister’s birth.
Heaven and Earth bestow auspicious signs,
And the village resounds with joy.
This month stands at the center,
Fitting to echo the ode of Song Gao’s birth in Shen.
May his years match the heavens,
And his longevity extend with the tripartite felicitations of Hua.
Such is the sincerity of our birthday prayers.

Thus, we prostrate ourselves before the Jade Emperor of the Luminous Heaven,
Whose august presence governs the ten directions,
Whose great deeds are established through kalpas uncounted.
No distance is too far, no nearness too close—
All equally bathed in his illumination.
The nine lands and all beings of blood and breath
Revere and serve none but him.

We now reverently proclaim with utmost sincerity: Your servant, dust-bound and impure, has served with trepidation day and night. Ashamed of my dullness and ignorance, how dare I presume to stand before the Most High, yet I fast, bathe, and purify myself to serve the Emperor. To respond to the Heavenly Presence—this is what is meant by the divine: all-hearing, all-seeing, upright, and just. With reverence in my station, I am fortunate to gaze upon the sun through parting clouds, as though treading on thin ice over an abyss. Though my prayers may go unheard, though my deeds may remain unseen, I stand before the Way of the Manifest. May the people prosper and flourish, may they grow old in wisdom, and may their blessings be bestowed.

Your servant, overwhelmed with awe, gazes toward the heavens and longs for the sagely presence with utmost urgency.

We now invoke the Immortal Hosts of the Three Primes, the assembled ranks of *pusa* officials, all the immortals gathered for this *jiao* rite, the City God and Lady of the Prefecture and County, the Lady of the Local Domain, the Ladies of the Golden Turtle’s various temples who bestow blessings, all *pusa* officials of this sanctuary, the Incense Officials of the Three Realms, and the Attendants of the Day—by the power of this true incense, we make universal offering.

This incense is the radiant splendor of jade blossoms, the purple qi congealed into mist, a fragrant cloud woven thick, ascending straight to the Nine Heavens. May the Golden Lads who attend the incense and the Jade Maidens who scatter flowers convey our petition, granting all as we beseech. With utmost devotion, we humbly submit our intent, looking up to your compassionate shade, that blessings may extend to all the people.

Now, as the altar of orchids opens the ritual, we bow our heads in reverence, taking refuge in the Boundless Great Dao.

*Chant:*
The assembly of the Dao altar, each turning their minds,
Take refuge in the Three Treasures, all reciting in unison.

*Cold Altar...*
*To the Perfected within the curtain...*
*Contending with Heaven and Earth...*
*Mystery within the Grotto...*
*Rise.*

The Firelight Dispelling Filth, Primordial Sovereign—
Kneeling before the censer:
*The Dao is cultivated through the heart...*
*The Five Stars’ incantation, the Five Stars arrayed in splendor.*

*Ignite the censer—*
*Strike the Dharma Drum twenty-four times.*

O Most High Three Heavens, Primordial Origin, First Three Qi, Most Exalted Lord Lao, summon forth from within our bodies the Three and Five Merit Officers, the Left and Right Incense Officials and Envoys, the Left and Right Dragon-Riding Couriers, the Golden Lads who attend the incense, the Jade Maidens who scatter flowers, the Twenty-Four Officers and Generals of the Five Directions and the Day—let them emerge with solemn dignity.

Let the local earth gods and domain deities of this place emerge. Your servant now, in the act of burning incense and performing the Dao, respectfully petitions on behalf of [name/purpose], with all sincerity as set forth in the written prayer. With this invocation, may the Primordial Qi of the Ten Directions’ True and Upright Ones descend and flow into our bodies, that our petition may swiftly reach the presence of the Queen Mother of the Nine Heavens, the August Empress of the Dao.

*Announce the Dharma Titles:*
The humble one now petitions the Queen Mother of the Nine Heavens, the August Empress of the Dao—
Her sacred station as before.

We reverently acknowledge that when the Three Powers first divided, the human way was established between Heaven and Earth. The sages of old were apportioned their offices, and the Emperor and Empress were entrusted with the registers of life and destiny. Humans, being most noble, hold a duty most exalted. They nurture the po and refine the form, beginning with the inscription of life at the Southern Culmen. They manifest good and punish evil, then assign destinies under the celestial palaces. We look up to the thirty-six august sovereigns, who truly govern the lives of countless beings. Wealth and poverty, nobility and lowliness are fixed at the moment of conception. Longevity and early death, short and long lives—all are held in their grasp. Above, they uphold the majestic commands of the celestial bureaus; below, they respond to the prayers of worldly descendants. Those born into families of accumulated virtue are blessed with wisdom and wealth, while those born after accumulated transgressions suffer lowliness and early demise. Their judgment is impartial, not a hair’s breadth swayed by favor. Yet if one turns a single thought toward refuge, the hundred spirits will surely witness it.

Now, with utmost reverence and devotion, we bow our heads in sincerity. Presuming to present the rites of this *jiao* offering, we bend every effort to express our earnest plea. We take refuge in the Thirty-Six Heavenly Emperors and Empresses above, and the divine attendants of the Sacred Aid Immortal Consorts. We humbly pray that you mount the clouds and ride the cranes, arraying your divine procession to descend. Ascend the void and ride the phoenix, answering the earnest prayers of mortals. The ritual assembly, with utmost devotion, takes refuge and makes this invocation.

Since the welcoming rites above and below have been performed, all the immortals of the inner and outer palaces have descended. We now request that the immortal ranks be arrayed with solemnity to receive the divine presence.

Your servant respectfully petitions.

May the Earth Kings, Radiant Kings, and the Venerable Mother of the Jambudvīpa World, the Six Perils Emperors and Empresses, in their Dao compassion, descend to take their thrones. May the Nine Heavens’ Inspecting and Investigating Holy Mother, the Demon-Quelling Empress; the Heavenly Net’s Registry-Holding Holy Mother, the Jade Perfection Empress; the Eight Directions’ Surveillance Holy Mother, the Golden Light Empress; the Southern Culmen’s Nurturing Holy Mother, the Fire Light Empress; the Eastern Culmen’s Life-Preserving Holy Mother, the Azure-Clad Empress; the Dharma-Governing and Virtue-Gathering Holy Mother, the Eight Directions’ Empress; the Earth Deity Empress who Upholds the Dao and Emulates Heaven; and the Primordial Empress of the Nine Heavens’ Dao Mother—having been invoked above, now grace us with their descent. With utmost devotion, the assembly offers this ritual service.

Within the jade hall, dragon thrones are arrayed—may all the heavens swiftly descend.
With a heart’s sincerity, we take refuge in the Great Dao; our prayers align with the mind’s intent.
Vases hold flowers wafting musk, censers’ smoke curls in fragrant tendrils.
Thrice we raise our wisdom in supplication, praying for profound blessings of grace.

*Step of Emptiness*
The precious throne descends upon the golden hall, its rosy crown gleaming in jade stillness.
Ten thousand immortals pay homage at the imperial abode, their flying slippers rooted in clouds of radiance.

*Hymn of Seated Peace*
The throne of the Nine Heavens, jade table and dragon seat,
Golden light illumines, a hundred treasures shine.
All heavens descend, the great and upright flourish.
Receiving this precious throne, may elder brothers know peace and tranquility.
Fire-pears and immortal dates,
Jade-like nectar peaches,
Jade flowers and wax candles,
Sweet dew and clarified butter,
Jade springs and auspicious dew,
Phoenix tea and dragon sprouts—
The heavenly kitchens’ fragrant offerings appear at thought’s bidding.

We have heard that when clarity and turbidity were first divided and yin and yang took their places,
Heaven and Earth conjoined to bear the Six Sons, and in their harmony nurtured all living beings.
How much more so the Primordial Empress of the Dao Mother,
Who alone upholds the teachings of yin.
Moreover, the wombs of the world below depend entirely on her sacred grace.
All mortal forms flow within the Three Realms, each a sign of the six yin’s inception.
Those who accumulate goodness see their descendants multiply;
Those who hoard evil watch their branches wither.
Every prayer is answered, no plea goes unheeded.
Bestow sons, and they shall be endowed with wisdom and intelligence;
Grant daughters, and they shall be blessed with beauty and grace.
In an instant, she rescues from life and death; in a fleeting moment, she dispels calamity.
Rewarding virtue and punishing excess, she holds to an unchanging decree.
Wielding the scales of rectitude, she repels evil and saves the lives of all beings.
When the Nine Spirits are revered, resonance is assured.

We, though unworthy, have been born as human beings and are fortunate to live in this flourishing age.
Following the Dao’s transformation through the various offices, we propagate the great Dharma in its numinous emptiness.
Thus, we purify the sacred altar and reverently invite the true lords.
Fragrant incense rises like a jeweled canopy, auspicious signs ascend before the jade hall’s terrace.
Flowers scatter like jade blossoms, their fragrance perfuming the Jade Capital’s mountain.
With hearts steadfast in sincerity, we reach the offering; through virtue, its fragrance spreads.
In gratitude for sacred grace, we confess our transgressions.
May she uphold us in perpetuity and safeguard childbearing without peril.
We array this splendid feast to extend our boundless blessings.

May auspicious light descend, and the holy consorts protect all living beings.
May the cloud-borne chariots deign to arrive, descending upon this ritual feast to witness our merit and virtue.
Through fragrant incense, we connect with the sublime; through utmost sincerity, we convey our devotion.
The sacred work is impartial, its luminous insight all-pervading.

Today, we pray that the present Emperor, Empress, and all officials
May enjoy longevity equal to heaven, their descendants flourishing day by day.
May their lineage’s distant origins flourish, their jade-like splendor ever radiant.
May their virtuous teachings spread beyond the shifting sands, and war cease in the northern deserts.
May the people delight in their labors, blessed with timely winds and rains.
May the barbarians of the north return to benevolence, and the frontier multitudes find peace.
May auspicious fungi be offered, and purple bamboo present its omens.
May all within the four seas and under heaven return to the Way.

We, in our presumption and temerity, bow our heads in reverence.
We offer incense, present tea, and pour wine in the initial libation.
Scatter flowers upon the clouds—
Before all the perfected, we make our offerings.

Again, we invoke the ranks of the Dharma, addressing the sacred thrones as before.

We have heard that at the center of the earth’s expanse lies the gathering place of all living beings,
And upon the earth’s body resides the revered deity who oversees destinies.
She governs the registers of life within the various palaces and oversees infants in their allotted lifespans.
She determines good and evil, granting or withholding as she deems fit.
She divides yin and yang, assigning gender—female or male.
Not a hair’s breadth is biased; every fate is fixed by measure.

Now, for so-and-so, who prays for myriad blessings to come and a thousand auspices to gather,
For descendants’ fortunes to flourish and households to prosper,
For generations of worthiness and hopes of boundless posterity—
We reverently beseech the Primordial Empress of the Nine Heavens’ Dao Mother, the Sacred Aid Immortal Consorts,
And the attendant immortals who uphold the registers of life, relying on their grace to safeguard birth.
Deliver and save the people of the world; may they live in peace and the age be redeemed.
Release the transgressions already recorded and protect nurturing without peril.

With utmost sincerity, we cultivate merit and virtue, lifting our prayers to beseech the compassionate shade’s shelter over the field of the self.

We humbly pray that the nine generations and seven ancestors, all karmic kin from past kalpas,
Be delivered from the dark paths and ascend to the blessed realms.
May their names be inscribed in the Southern Palace’s register of life, their transgressions erased from the Northern Bureau’s ledger of faults.
Bestowed with sacred peaches, may they extend their years to three thousand;
Granted fiery jujubes, may their lifespans stretch across ten epochs.
May all kin, near and far, equally receive this sheltering grace.

The officiant, with reverent devotion, offers incense, presents tea, and pours wine—now performing the second libation—though this crimson heart holds no worthy offering.

Reverently invoking the sacred ranks,
[Officiant’s title and address as before,]
We prostrate and declare:

We have heard that the great deities of the Four Waterways truly govern the gathering of life,
While the vital qi of the Five Peaks transcribes the finest essence into humanity.
Though the watery palaces lie in distant obscurity, they are the very ground where infants take form—
No plea goes unanswered, no supplication unheeded.

Now, for so-and-so, who truly relies on this boundless grace,
May deepest wishes be eternally fulfilled, blessings flow to descendants, and prosperity extend through the lineage’s roots and branches.
May sons all attain wealth and nobility with keen intelligence,
And daughters be virtuous and fair, blessed with auspicious countenance.
May no evil defile them, no illness assail them,
All equally cherished by nurturing kindness, each rejoicing in the joy of life’s fulfillment.

Relying on this single thought of devotion, we look up to the merciful ones for their radiant witness.

Reverently beseeching...

To the Celestial Dao Mother, Supreme Empress of the Primordial Origin, and the Divine Consort of Numinous Salvation, with their attendant immortals—

We humbly pray that in the Jade Terrace’s halls, past transgressions from former kalpas be absolved, and in the Trāyastriṃśa heavens, blessings and emoluments be bestowed upon this present life. May the lineage flourish for a hundred generations, rich in prosperity and blessed with many sons. May distant descendants multiply like spreading branches, their clans expanding in kinship. May peace and felicity be preserved, mother and child untroubled. May no evil assail them, and may the hundred spirits ever guard them.

We, unworthy as we are, dare to trespass upon your grace again and again, prostrating ourselves in utmost reverence. We offer incense, present tea, pour wine, and humbly dedicate these offerings. We scatter flowers. All assembled in this Daoist ritual, each with sincere heart, chant and recite according to the proper rites. The *Scripture of the Southern Culmen on Bestowing Life* is now concluded. The memorial is solemnly proclaimed in gratitude.

The preceding petition has been respectfully presented. The sagely nature is impartial—surely it will deign to witness and respond. Now, with another offering of precious incense, we reverently address the Celestial Dao Mother, Supreme Empress of the Primordial Origin, the Divine Consort of Numinous Salvation, and all the perfected lords of this rite.

We have heard that when yin and yang converge, the myriad beings take form; when heaven and earth intermingle in primordial qi, the hosts of spirits manifest their signs.
